   (part) => {\n            clearTimeout(id)\n            resolve(part)\n          },\n          (err) => {\n            clearTimeout(id)\n            reject(err)\n          },\n        )\n      })\n\n      if (part.done) {\n        ctrl.close()\n        return\n      }\n\n      ctrl.enqueue(part.value)\n    },\n    async cancel(reason) {\n      ctl.abort(reason)\n      await      })\n      const ok =\n        hasKey ||\n        Boolean(yield* dep.auth(input.id)) ||\n        Boolean((yield* dep.config()).provider?.[\"opencode\"]?.options?.apiKey)\n\n      if (!ok) {\n },\n  }\n  if (c?.context_over_200k) {\n    result.experimentalOver200K = {\n      cache: {\n        read: c.context_over_200k.cache_read ?? 0,\n        write: c.context_over_200k.cache_write ?? 0,\n      },\n      input: c.context_over_200k.input,\n      output: c.context_over_200k.output,\n    }\n  }\n  return result\n}\n\nfunction fromModelsDevModel(provider: ModelsDev.Provider, model: id: model.id,\n      url: model.provider?.api ?? provider.api ?? \"\",\n      npm: model.provider?.npm ?? provider.npm ?? \"@ai-sdk/openai-compatible\",\n    },\n    status: model.status ?? },\n    capabilities: {\n      temperature: model.temperature ?? false,\n      reasoning: model.reasoning ?? false,\n      attachment: model.attachment ?? false,\n      toolcall: model.tool_call ?? model.modalities?.output?.includes(\"image\") ?? false,\n        video: model.modalities?.output?.includes(\"video\") ?? false,\n        pdf: model.modalities?.output?.includes(\"pdf\") ?? false,\n      },\n      interleaved: model.interleaved ?? false,\n    },\n    release_date: model.release_date ?? \"\",\n    variants: {},\n  }\n\n  return {\n    ...base,\n    variants: mapValues(ProviderTransform.variants(base), (v) => v),\n  }\n}\n\nexport function fromModelsDevProvider(provider: ModelsDev.Provider): Info {\n  const models: Record<string, Model> = {}\n  for (const [key, model] of Object.entries(provider.models)) {\n    models[key] = fromModelsDevModel(provider, model)\n    for (const [mode, opts] of Object.entries(model.experimental?.modes ?? {})) {\n [],\n    options: {},\n    models,\n  }\n}\n\nconst layer: Layer.Layer<\n  Service,\n  never,\n  Config.Service | Auth.Service | Plugin.Service | AppFileSystem.Service | Env.Service\n> =    function mergeProvider(providerID: ProviderID, provider: Partial<Info>) {\n          const existing = providers[providerID]\n          if (existing) {\n            // @ts-expect-error\n            providers[providerID] = mergeDeep(existing, provider)\n            return\n          }\n          const match = database[providerID]\n          if (!match) return\n          // @ts-expect-error\n          providers[providerID] = mergeDeep(match, provider)\n        }\n\n        // load plugins first so config() hook runs before reading cfg.provider\n        const plugins = yield* plugin.list()\n\n        // now read config providers - includes any modifications from plugin config() hook\n        const configProviders = Object.entries(cfg.provider ?? {})\n        const disabled = new [])\n        const enabled = cfg.enabled_providers ? new Set(cfg.enabled_providers) : null\n\n        function isProviderAllowed(providerID: ProviderID): boolean {\n          if (enabled && !enabled.has(providerID)) return false\n          if (disabled.has(providerID)) return false\n          return true\n        }\n\n        // extend database from config\n        for (const [providerID, provider] of configProviders) {\n          const existing = database[providerID]\n          const parsed: Info = {\n            id: ProviderID.make(providerID),\n            name: provider.name ?? existing?.name ?? providerID,\n            env: provider.env ?? existing?.env ??            id: ModelID.make(modelID),\n              api: {\n                id: model.id ?? existingModel?.api.id ?? modelID,\n                npm:\n                  model.provider?.npm ??\n           name,\n              providerID: ProviderID.make(providerID),\n              capabilities: {\n                temperature: model.temperature ?? existingModel?.capabilities.temperature ??          },\n              cost: {\n                input: model?.cost?.input ?? existingModel?.cost?.input ?? 0,\n                output: model?.cost?.output ?? existingModel?.cost?.output ?? 0,\n                cache: {\n                  read: model?.cost?.cache_read ?? existingModel?.cost?.cache.read ?? 0,\n                  write: model?.cost?.cache_write ?? existingModel?.cost?.cache.write ?? existingModel?.limit?.context ?? 0,\n                input: model.limit?.input ?? existingModel?.limit?.input,\n                output: model.limit?.output ?? existingModel?.limit?.output ?? 0,\n              },\n              headers: mergeDeep(existingModel?.headers ?? {}, model.headers ?? {}),\n              family: model.family ?? existingModel?.family ?? \"\",\n              release_date:     })\n        }\n\n        // load apikeys\n        const auths = yield* auth.all().pipe(Effect.orDie)\n        for (const [id, provider] of Object.entries(auths)) {\n          const providerID = }\n          if (provider.env) partial.env = provider.env\n          if (provider.name) partial.name = provider.name\n          if (provider.options) partial.options = provider.options\n          mergeProvider(providerID, partial)\n        }\n\n        const gitlab = ProviderID.make(\"gitlab\")\n        if (discoveryLoaders[gitlab] && providers[gitlab] && isProviderAllowed(gitlab)) {\n log.warn(\"state discovery error\", { id: \"gitlab\", error: e })\n            }\n          })\n        }\n\n        for (const hook of plugins) {\n          const p = hook.provider\n          const models = p?.models\n          if (!p || !models) continue\n\n          const providerID = ProviderID.make(p.id)\n          if (disabled.has(providerID)) continue\n\n          const provider = {\n            const next = await models(provider, { auth: pluginAuth })\n            return Object.fromEntries(\n              Object.entries(next).map(([id, model]) => [\n                id,\n                {\n                  ...model,\n                  id: ModelID.make(id),\n                  providerID,\n                },\n              ]),\n            )\n          })\n        }\n\n providers[providerID]\n            continue\n          }\n\n          const configProvider = cfg.provider?.[providerID]\n\n          for (const [modelID, model] of Object.entries(provider.models)) {\n            model.api.id = model.api.id ?? model.id ?? modelID\n            if (\n              modelID === \"gpt-5-chat-latest\" ||\n              (providerID === ProviderID.openrouter && modelID === \"openai/gpt-5-chat\")\n            )\n              delete provider.models[modelID]\n            if (model.status === \"alpha\" && !Flag.OPENCODE_ENABLE_EXPERIMENTAL_MODELS) delete configProvider.blacklist.includes(modelID)) ||\n              (configProvider?.whitelist && !configProvider.whitelist.includes(modelID))\n            )\n              delete function resolveSDK(model: Model, s: State, envs: Record<string, string | undefined>) {\n      try {\n        using _ = log.time(\"getSDK\", {\n          providerID: model.providerID,\n        })\n        const provider = s.providers[model.providerID]\n        const options = { ...provider.options }\n\n        if (model.providerID === \"google-vertex\" && !model.api.npm.includes(\"@ai-sdk/openai-compatible\")) {\n          delete options.fetch\n        }\n\n        if (model.api.npm.includes(\"@ai-sdk/openai-compatible\") && options[\"includeUsage\"] !== false) {\n          options[\"includeUsage\"] = true\n        }\n\n        const baseURL = iife(() => {\n          let url =\n            typeof options[\"baseURL\"] === \"string\" && options[\"baseURL\"] !== \"\" ? options[\"baseURL\"] : model.api.url\n          if (!url) return\n\n          const loader = s.varsLoaders[model.providerID]\n          if (loader) {\n            const vars = loader(options)\n            for (const [key, value] of Object.entries(vars)) {\n              const field = \"${\" + key + \"}\"\n              url = url.replaceAll(field, value)\n            }\n          }\n\n          url = url.replace(/\\$\\{([^}]+)\\}/g, (item, key) => {\n            const val = envs[String(key)]\n            return val ?? item\n          })\n          return url\n        })\n\n        if (baseURL !== undefined) options[\"baseURL\"] = baseURL\n        if (options[\"apiKey\"] === undefined && provider.key) options[\"apiKey\"] = provider.key\n        if (model.headers)\n          options[\"headers\"] = {\n            ...options[\"headers\"],\n            ...model.headers,\n          }\n\n        const key = Hash.fast(\n          JSON.stringify({\n            providerID: model.providerID,\n            npm: model.api.npm,\n            options,\n          }),\n        )\n        const existing = s.sdk.get(key)\n        if (existing) return existing\n\n        const customFetch = options[\"fetch\"]\n        const chunkTimeout = options[\"chunkTimeout\"]\n        delete options[\"chunkTimeout\"]\n\n        options[\"fetch\"] = async (input: any, init?: BunFetchRequestInit) => {\n          const fetchFn = customFetch ?? fetch\n          const opts = init ?? {}\n          const chunkAbortCtl = typeof chunkTimeout === \"number\" && chunkTimeout > 0 ? new AbortController() : undefined\n          const signals: AbortSignal[] = []\n\n          if (opts.signal) signals.push(opts.signal)\n          if (chunkAbortCtl) signals.push(chunkAbortCtl.signal)\n          if (options[\"timeout\"] !== undefined && options[\"timeout\"] !== null && options[\"timeout\"] !== false)\n            signals.push(AbortSignal.timeout(options[\"timeout\"]))\n\n          const combined = signals.length === 0 ? null : signals.length === 1 ? signals[0] : AbortSignal.any(signals)\n          if (combined) opts.signal = combined\n\n          // Strip openai itemId metadata following what codex does\n          if (model.api.npm === \"@ai-sdk/openai\" && opts.body && opts.method === \"POST\") {\n            const body = JSON.parse(opts.body as string)\n            const isAzure = model.providerID.includes(\"azure\")\n            const keepIds = isAzure && body.store === true\n            if (!keepIds && Array.isArray(body.input)) {\n              for (const item of body.input) {\n                if (\"id\" in item) {\n                  delete item.id\n                }\n              }\n              opts.body = JSON.stringify(body)\n            }\n          }\n\n          const res = await fetchFn(input, {\n            ...opts,\n            // @ts-ignore see here: https://github.com/oven-sh/bun/issues/16682\n            timeout: false,\n          })\n\n          if (!chunkAbortCtl) return res\n          return wrapSSE(res, chunkTimeout, chunkAbortCtl)\n        }\n\n        const bundledLoader = BUNDLED_PROVIDERS[model.api.npm]\n        if (bundledLoader) {\n          log.info(\"using bundled provider\", {\n            providerID: model.providerID,\n            pkg: model.api.npm,\n          })\n          const factory = await bundledLoader()\n          const loaded = factory({\n            name: model.providerID,\n            ...options,\n          })\n          s.sdk.set(key, loaded)\n          return loaded as SDK\n        }\n\n        let installedPath: string\n        if (!model.api.npm.startsWith(\"file://\")) {\n          const item = await Npm.add(model.api.npm)\n          if (!item.entrypoint) throw new Error(`Package ${model.api.npm} has no import entrypoint`)\n          installedPath = item.entrypoint\n        } else {\n          log.info(\"loading local provider\", { pkg: model.api.npm })\n          installedPath = model.api.npm\n        }\n\n        // `installedPath` is a local entry path or an existing `file://` URL. Normalize\n        // only path inputs so Node on Windows accepts the dynamic import.\n        const importSpec = installedPath.startsWith(\"file://\") ? installedPath : pathToFileURL(installedPath).href\n        const mod = await import(importSpec)\n\n        const fn = mod[Object.keys(mod).find((key) => key.startsWith(\"create\"))!]\n        const loaded = fn({\n          name: model.providerID,\n          ...options,\n        })\n        s.sdk.set(key, loaded)\n        return loaded as SDK\n      } catch (e) {\n        throw new InitError({ providerID: model.providerID }, { cause: e })\n      }\n    }\n\n    const getProvider = Effect.fn(\"Provider.getProvider\")((providerID: ProviderID) =>\n      InstanceState.use(state, (s) => s.providers[providerID]),\n    )\n\n    const getModel = Effect.fn(\"Provider.getModel\")(function* (providerID: ProviderID, modelID: ModelID) {\n      const s = yield* InstanceState.get(state)\n      const provider = s.providers[providerID]\n      if (!provider) {\n        const available = Object.keys(s.providers)\n        const matches = fuzzysort.go(providerID, available, { limit: 3, threshold: -10000 })\n        throw new ModelNotFoundError({ providerID, modelID, suggestions: matches.map((m) => m.target) })\n      }\n\n      const info = provider.models[modelID]\n      if (!info) {\n        const available = Object.keys(provider.models)\n        const matches = fuzzysort.go(modelID, available, { limit: 3, threshold: -10000 })\n        throw new ModelNotFoundError({ providerID, modelID, suggestions: matches.map((m) => m.target) })\n      }\n      return info\n    })\n\n    const getLanguage = Effect.fn(\"Provider.getLanguage\")(function* (model: Model) {\n      const s = yield* InstanceState.get(state)\n      const envs = yield* env.all()\n      const key = `${model.providerID}/${model.id}`\n      if (s.models.has(key)) return s.models.get(key)!\n\n      return yield* Effect.promise(async () => {\n        const provider = s.providers[model.providerID]\n        const sdk = await resolveSDK(model, s, envs)\n\n        try {\n          const language = s.modelLoaders[model.providerID]\n            ? await s.modelLoaders[model.providerID](sdk, model.api.id, {\n                ...provider.options,\n                ...model.options,\n              })\n            : sdk.languageModel(model.api.id)\n          s.models.set(key, language)\n          return language\n        } catch (e) {\n          if (e instanceof NoSuchModelError)\n            throw new ModelNotFoundError(\n              {\n                modelID: model.id,\n                providerID: model.providerID,\n              },\n              { cause: e },\n            )\n          throw e\n        }\n      })\n    })\n\n    const closest = Effect.fn(\"Provider.closest\")(function* (providerID: ProviderID, query: string[]) {\n      const s = yield* InstanceState.get(state)\n      const provider = s.providers[providerID]\n      if (!provider) return undefined\n      for (const item of query) {\n        for (const modelID of Object.keys(provider.models)) {\n          if (modelID.includes(item)) return { providerID, modelID }\n        }\n      }\n      return undefined\n    })\n\n    const getSmallModel = Effect.fn(\"Provider.getSmallModel\")(function* (providerID: ProviderID) {\n      const cfg = yield* config.get()\n\n      if (cfg.small_model) {\n        const parsed = parseModel(cfg.small_model)\n        return yield* getModel(parsed.providerID, parsed.modelID)\n      }\n\n      const s = yield* InstanceState.get(state)\n      const provider = s.providers[providerID]\n      if (!provider) return undefined\n\n      let priority = [\n        \"claude-haiku-4-5\",\n        \"claude-haiku-4.5\",\n        \"3-5-haiku\",\n        \"3.5-haiku\",\n        \"gemini-3-flash\",\n        \"gemini-2.5-flash\",\n        \"gpt-5-nano\",\n      ]\n      if (providerID.startsWith(\"opencode\")) {\n        priority = [\"gpt-5-nano\"]\n      }\n      if (providerID.startsWith(\"github-copilot\")) {\n        priority = [\"gpt-5-mini\", \"claude-haiku-4.5\", ...priority]\n      }\n      for (const item of priority) {\n        if (providerID === ProviderID.amazonBedrock) {\n          const crossRegionPrefixes = [\"global.\", \"us.\", \"eu.\"]\n          const candidates = Object.keys(provider.models).filter((m) => m.includes(item))\n\n          const globalMatch = candidates.find((m) => m.startsWith(\"global.\"))\n          if (globalMatch) return yield* getModel(providerID, ModelID.make(globalMatch))\n\n          const region = provider.options?.region\n          if (region) {\n            const regionPrefix = region.split(\"-\")[0]\n            if (regionPrefix === \"us\" || regionPrefix === \"eu\") {\n              const regionalMatch = candidates.find((m) => m.startsWith(`${regionPrefix}.`))\n              if (regionalMatch) return yield* getModel(providerID, ModelID.make(regionalMatch))\n            }\n          }\n\n          const unprefixed = candidates.find((m) => !crossRegionPrefixes.some((p) => m.startsWith(p)))\n          if (unprefixed) return yield* getModel(providerID, ModelID.make(unprefixed))\n        } else {\n          for (const model of Object.keys(provider.models)) {\n            if (model.includes(item)) return yield* getModel(providerID, ModelID.make(model))\n          }\n        }\n      }\n\n      return undefined\n    })\n\n    const defaultModel = Effect.fn(\"Provider.defaultModel\")(function* () {\n      const cfg = yield* config.get()\n      if (cfg.model) return parseModel(cfg.model)\n\n      const s = yield* InstanceState.get(state)\n      const recent = yield* fs.readJson(path.join(Global.Path.state, \"model.json\")).pipe(\n        Effect.map((x): { providerID: ProviderID; modelID: ModelID }[] => {\n          if (!isRecord(x) || !Array.isArray(x.recent)) return []\n          return x.recent.flatMap((item) => {\n            if (!isRecord(item)) return []\n            if (typeof item.providerID !== \"string\") return []\n 		"content": "import { APICallError } from \"ai\"\nimport { STATUS_CODES } from \"http\"\nimport { iife } from \"@/util/iife\"\nimport type { ProviderID } from \"./schema\"\n\n// Adapted from overflow detection patterns in:\n// https://github.com/badlogic/pi-mono/blob/main/packages/ai/src/utils/overflow.ts\nconst OVERFLOW_PATTERNS = [\n  /prompt is too long/i, // Anthropic\n  /input is too long for requested model/i, // Amazon Bedrock\n  /exceeds the context window/i, // OpenAI (Completions + Responses API message text)\n  /input token count.*exceeds the maximum/i, // Google (Gemini)\n  /maximum prompt length is \\d+/i, // xAI (Grok)\n  /reduce the length of the messages/i, // Groq\n  /maximum context length is \\d+ tokens/i, // OpenRouter, DeepSeek, vLLM\n  /exceeds the limit of \\d+/i, // GitHub Copilot\n  /exceeds the available context size/i, // llama.cpp server\n  /greater than the context length/i, // LM Studio\n  /context window exceeds limit/i, // MiniMax\n  /exceeded model token limit/i, // Kimi For Coding, Moonshot\n  /context[_ ]length[_ ]exceeded/i, // Generic fallback\n  /request entity too large/i, // HTTP 413\n  /context length is only \\d+ tokens/i, // vLLM\n  /input length.*exceeds.*context length/i, // vLLM\n  /prompt too long; exceeded (?:max )?context length/i, // Ollama explicit overflow error\n  /too large for model with \\d+ maximum context length/i, // Mistral\n  /model_context_window_exceeded/i, // z.ai non-standard finish_reason surfaced as error text\n]\n\nfunction isOpenAiErrorRetryable(e: APICallError) {\n  const status = e.statusCode\n  if (!status) return e.isRetryable\n  // openai sometimes returns 404 for models that are actually available\n  return status === 404 || e.isRetryable\n}\n\n// Providers not reliably handled in this function:\n// - z.ai: can accept overflow silently (needs token-count/context-window checks)\nfunction isOverflow(message: string) {\n  if (OVERFLOW_PATTERNS.some((p) => p.test(message))) return true\n\n  // Providers/status patterns handled outside of regex list:\n  // - Cerebras: often returns \"400 (no body)\" / \"413 (no body)\"\n  // - Mistral: often returns \"400 (no body)\" / \"413 (no body)\"\n  return /^4(00|13)\\s*(status code)?\\s*\\(no body\\)/i.test(message)\n}\n\nfunction message(providerID: ProviderID, e: APICallError) {\n  return iife(() => {\n    const msg = e.message\n    if (msg === \"\") {\n      if (e.responseBody) return e.responseBody\n      if (e.statusCode) {\n        const err = STATUS_CODES[e.statusCode]\n        if (err) return err\n      }\n      return \"Unknown error\"\n    }\n\n    if (!e.responseBody || (e.statusCode && msg !== STATUS_CODES[e.statusCode])) {\n      return msg\n    }\n\n    try {\n      const body = JSON.parse(e.responseBody)\n      // try to extract common error message fields\n      const errMsg = body.message || body.error || body.error?.message\n      if (errMsg && typeof errMsg === \"string\") {\n        return `${msg}: ${errMsg}`\n      }\n    } catch {}\n\n    // If responseBody is HTML (e.g. from a gateway or proxy error page),\n    // provide a human-readable message instead of dumping raw markup\n    if (/^\\s*<!doctype|^\\s*<html/i.test(e.responseBody)) {\n      if (e.statusCode === 401) {\n        return \"Unauthorized: request was blocked by a gateway or proxy. Your authentication token may be missing or expired — try running `opencode auth login <your provider URL>` to re-authenticate.\"\n      }\n      if (e.statusCode === 403) {\n        return \"Forbidden: request was blocked by a gateway or proxy. You may not have permission to access this resource — check your account and provider settings.\"\n      }\n      return msg\n    }\n\n    return `${msg}: ${e.responseBody}`\n  }).trim()\n}\n\nfunction json(input: unknown) {\n  if (typeof input === \"string\") {\n    try {\n      const result = JSON.parse(input)\n      if (result && typeof result === \"object\") return result\n      return undefined\n    } catch {\n      return undefined\n    }\n  }\n  if (typeof input === \"object\" && input !== null) {\n    return input\n  }\n  return undefined\n}\n\nexport type ParsedStreamError =\n  | {\n      type: \"context_overflow\"\n      message: string\n      responseBody: string\n    }\n  | {\n      type: \"api_error\"\n      message: string\n      isRetryable: false\n      responseBody: string\n    }\n\nexport function parseStreamError(input: unknown): ParsedStreamError | undefined {\n  const body = json(input)\n  if (!body) return\n\n  const responseBody = JSON.stringify(body)\n  if (body.type !== \"error\") return\n\n  switch (body?.error?.code) {\n    case \"context_length_exceeded\":\n      return {\n        type: \"context_overflow\",\n        message: \"Input exceeds context window of this model\",\n        responseBody,\n      }\n    case \"insufficient_quota\":\n      return {\n        type: \"api_error\",\n        message: \"Quota exceeded. Check your plan and billing details.\",\n        isRetryable: false,\n        responseBody,\n      }\n    case \"usage_not_included\":\n      return {\n        type: \"api_error\",\n        message: \"To use Codex with your ChatGPT plan, upgrade to Plus: https://chatgpt.com/explore/plus.\",\n        isRetryable: false,\n        responseBody,\n      }\n    case \"invalid_prompt\":\n      return {\n        type: \"api_error\",\n        message: typeof body?.error?.message === \"string\" ? body?.error?.message : \"Invalid prompt.\",\n        isRetryable: false,\n        responseBody,\n      }\n  }\n}\n\nexport type ParsedAPICallError =\n  | {\n      type: \"context_overflow\"\n      message: string\n      responseBody?: string\n    }\n  | {\n      type: \"api_error\"\n      message: string\n      statusCode?: number\n      isRetryable: boolean\n      responseHeaders?: Record<string, string>\n      responseBody?: string\n      metadata?: Record<string, string>\n    }\n\nexport function parseAPICallError(input: { providerID: ProviderID; error: APICallError }): ParsedAPICallError {\n  const m = message(input.providerID, input.error)\n  const body = json(input.error.responseBody)\n  if (isOverflow(m) || input.error.statusCode === 413 || body?.error?.code === \"context_length_exceeded\") {\n    return {\n      type: \"context_overflow\",\n      message: m,\n      responseBody: input.error.responseBody,\n    }\n  }\n\n  const metadata = input.error.url ? { url: input.error.url } : undefined\n  return {\n    type: \"api_error\",\n    message: m,\n    statusCode: input.error.statusCode,\n    isRetryable: input.providerID.startsWith(\"openai\") ? isOpenAiErrorRetryable(input.error) : input.error.isRetryable,\n    responseHeaders: input.error.responseHeaders,\n    responseBody: input.error.responseBody,\n    metadata,\n  }\n}\n",

\"zod/v4/core\"\nimport type * as Provider from \"./provider\"\nimport type * as ModelsDev from \"./models\"\nimport { iife } from \"@/util/iife\"\nimport { Flag } from \"@/flag/flag\"\n\ntype Modality = NonNullable<ModelsDev.Model[\"modalities\"]>[\"input\"][number]\n\nfunction mimeToModality(mime: string): Modality | undefined {\n  if (mime.startsWith(\"image/\")) return \"image\"\n  if (mime.startsWith(\"audio/\")) return \"audio\"\n  if (mime.startsWith(\"video/\")) return \"video\"\n  if (mime === \"application/pdf\") return \"pdf\"\n  return undefined\n}\n\nexport const OUTPUT_TOKEN_MAX = Flag.OPENCODE_EXPERIMENTAL_OUTPUT_TOKEN_MAX || 32_000\n\n// Maps npm package to the key the AI SDK expects for providerOptions\nfunction sdkKey(npm: string): string | undefined {\n  switch (npm) {\n    case \"@ai-sdk/github-copilot\":\n      return \"copilot\"\n    case \"@ai-sdk/azure\":\n      return \"azure\"\n    case \"@ai-sdk/openai\":\n      return \"openai\"\n    case \"@ai-sdk/amazon-bedrock\":\n      return \"bedrock\"\n    case \"@ai-sdk/anthropic\":\n    case \"@ai-sdk/google-vertex/anthropic\":\n      return \"anthropic\"\n    case \"@ai-sdk/google-vertex\":\n      return \"vertex\"\n    case \"@ai-sdk/google\":\n      return \"google\"\n    case \"@ai-sdk/deepseek\":\n      return \"deepseek\"\n    case \"@ai-sdk/gateway\":\n      return \"gateway\"\n    case \"@openrouter/ai-sdk-provider\":\n      return \"openrouter\"\n  }\n  return undefined\n}\n\n// Returns the providerOptions key that the AI SDK expects for the given model.\n// Note: @ai-sdk/openai-compatible's getOpenAIMetadata() hardcodes \"openaiCompatible\"\n// as the providerOptions key (see node_modules/@ai-sdk/openai-compatible/dist/index.mjs),\n// so we must use that key regardless of the provider's instantiated name.\nfunction providerOptionsKey(model: Provider.Model): string {\n  // @ai-sdk/openai-compatible's getOpenAIMetadata() hardcodes \"openaiCompatible\"\n  // as the providerOptions key for reasoning content. Any provider wrapping\n  // openai-compatible (e.g., @openrouter/ai-sdk-provider) inherits this behavior.\n  const npm = model.api.npm\n  if (npm === \"@ai-sdk/openai-compatible\" || npm === \"@openrouter/ai-sdk-provider\") {\n    return \"openaiCompatible\"\n  }\n  return sdkKey(npm) ?? \"openaiCompatible\"\n}\n\nfunction normalizeMessages(\n  msgs: ModelMessage[],\n  model: Provider.Model,\n  _options: Record<string, unknown>,\n): ModelMessage[] {\n  // Anthropic rejects messages with empty content - filter out empty string messages\n  // and remove empty text/reasoning parts from array content\n  if (model.api.npm === \"@ai-sdk/anthropic\" || model.api.npm === \"@ai-sdk/amazon-bedrock\") {\n    msgs = msgs\n      .map((msg) => {\n        if (typeof msg.content === \"string\") {\n          if (msg.content === \"\") return undefined\n          return msg\n        }\n        if (!Array.isArray(msg.content)) return msg\n        const filtered = msg.content.filter((part) => {\n          if (part.type === \"text\" || part.type === \"reasoning\") {\n            return part.text !== \"\"\n          }\n          return true\n        })\n        if (filtered.length === 0) return undefined\n        return { ...msg, content: filtered }\n      })\n      .filter((msg): msg is ModelMessage => msg !== undefined && msg.content !== \"\")\n  }\n\n  if (model.api.id.includes(\"claude\")) {\n    const scrub = (id: string) => id.replace(/[^a-zA-Z0-9_-]/g, \"_\")\n    msgs = msgs.map((msg) => {\n      if (msg.role === \"assistant\" && Array.isArray(msg.content)) {\n        return {\n          ...msg,\n          content: msg.content.map((part) => {\n            if (part.type === \"tool-call\" || part.type === \"tool-result\") {\n              return { ...part, toolCallId: scrub(part.toolCallId) }\n            }\n            return part\n          }),\n        }\n      }\n      if (msg.role === \"tool\" && Array.isArray(msg.content)) {\n        return {\n          ...msg,\n          content: msg.content.map((part) => {\n            if (part.type === \"tool-result\") {\n              return { ...part, toolCallId: scrub(part.toolCallId) }\n            }\n            return part\n          }),\n        }\n      }\n      return msg\n    })\n  }\n  if ([\"@ai-sdk/anthropic\", \"@ai-sdk/google-vertex/anthropic\"].includes(model.api.npm)) {\n    // Anthropic rejects assistant turns where tool_use blocks are followed by non-tool\n    // content, e.g. [tool_use, tool_use, text], with:\n    // `tool_use` ids were found without `tool_result` blocks immediately after...\n    //\n    // Reorder that invalid shape into [text] + [tool_use, tool_use]. Consecutive\n    // assistant messages are later merged by the provider/SDK, so preserving the\n    // original [tool_use...] then [text] order still produces the invalid payload.\n    //\n    // The root cause appears to be somewhere upstream where the stream is originally\n    // processed. We were unable to locate an exact narrower reproduction elsewhere,\n    // so we keep this transform in place for the time being.\n    msgs = msgs.flatMap((msg) => {\n      if (msg.role !== \"assistant\" || !Array.isArray(msg.content)) return [msg]\n\n      const parts = msg.content\n      const first = parts.findIndex((part) => part.type === \"tool-call\")\n      if (first === -1) return [msg]\n      if (!parts.slice(first).some((part) => part.type !== \"tool-call\")) return [msg]\n      return [\n        { ...msg, content: parts.filter((part) => part.type !== \"tool-call\") },\n        { ...msg, content: parts.filter((part) => part.type === \"tool-call\") },\n      ]\n    })\n  }\n  if (\n    model.providerID === \"mistral\" ||\n    model.api.id.toLowerCase().includes(\"mistral\") ||\n    model.api.id.toLocaleLowerCase().includes(\"devstral\")\n  ) {\n    const scrub = (id: string) => {\n      return id\n        .replace(/[^a-zA-Z0-9]/g, \"\") // Remove non-alphanumeric characters\n        .substring(0, 9) // Take first 9 characters\n        .padEnd(9, \"0\") // Pad with zeros if less than 9 characters\n    }\n    const result: ModelMessage[] = []\n    for (let i = 0; i < msgs.length; i++) {\n      const msg = msgs[i]\n      const nextMsg = msgs[i + 1]\n\n      if (msg.role === \"assistant\" && Array.isArray(msg.content)) {\n        msg.content = msg.content.map((part) => {\n          if (part.type === \"tool-call\" || part.type === \"tool-result\") {\n            return { ...part, toolCallId: scrub(part.toolCallId) }\n          }\n          return part\n        })\n      }\n      if (msg.role === \"tool\" && Array.isArray(msg.content)) {\n        msg.content = msg.content.map((part) => {\n          if (part.type === \"tool-result\") {\n            return { ...part, toolCallId: scrub(part.toolCallId) }\n          }\n          return part\n        })\n      }\n      result.push(msg)\n\n      // Fix message sequence: tool messages cannot be followed by user messages\n      if (msg.role === \"tool\" && nextMsg?.role === \"user\") {\n        result.push({\n          role: \"assistant\",\n          content: [\n            {\n              type: \"text\",\n              text: \"Done.\",\n            },\n          ],\n        })\n      }\n    }\n    return result\n  }\n\n  // Detect whether the model uses reasoning/thinking and determine the\n  // providerOptions key/field for reasoning_content. For models without\n  // interleaved configured (e.g., DeepSeek via @ai-sdk/openai-compatible),\n  // default to the OpenAI-compatible reasoning_content field.\n  const interleaved = model.capabilities.interleaved\n  const isInterleaved = typeof interleaved === \"object\" && interleaved.field\n  const field = isInterleaved ? interleaved.field : \"reasoning_content\"\n  const key = providerOptionsKey(model)\n\n  // Check if we need to handle reasoning parts:\n  // - interleaved explicitly configured, OR\n  // - model has reasoning capability, OR\n  // - messages already contain reasoning parts (from DB replay)\n  const hasReasoningContent =\n    isInterleaved ||\n    model.capabilities.reasoning ||\n    msgs.some((msg) =>\n      msg.role === \"assistant\" &&\n      Array.isArray(msg.content) &&\n      msg.content.some((part: any) => part.type === \"reasoning\"),\n    )\n\n  if (hasReasoningContent) {\n    // @ai-sdk/deepseek 原生处理 reasoning，不走 providerOptions 注入。\n    // convertToDeepSeekChatMessages() 直接从 content 中读取 reasoning part，\n    // 不要剥离，保留在 content 数组里。\n    if (model.api.npm === \"@ai-sdk/deepseek\") {\n      return msgs.map((msg) => ({\n        ...msg,\n        providerOptions: {\n          ...msg.providerOptions,\n          [key]: {\n            ...msg.providerOptions?.[key],\n            thinking: { type: \"enabled\" },\n          },\n        },\n      }))\n    }\n\n    return msgs.map((msg) => {\n      if (msg.role === \"assistant\" && Array.isArray(msg.content)) {\n        const reasoningParts = msg.content.filter((part: any) => part.type === \"reasoning\")\n        const reasoningText = reasoningParts.map((part: any) => part.text).join(\"\")\n\n        // Filter out reasoning parts from content\n        const filteredContent = msg.content.filter((part: any) => part.type !== \"reasoning\")\n\n        // DeepSeek reasoning API requires ALL assistant messages in the conversation\n        // history to carry reasoning_content (even empty string). Old DB-replayed\n        // messages may have no reasoning parts at all — inject empty string for those.\n        return {\n          ...msg,\n          content: filteredContent,\n          providerOptions: {\n            ...msg.providerOptions,\n            [key]: {\n              ...msg.providerOptions?.[key],\n              [field]: reasoningText || \"\",\n            },\n          },\n        }\n      }\n\n      // Also handle string-content assistant messages (old DB format).\n      // Inject empty reasoning_content to satisfy DeepSeek API requirement.\n      if (msg.role === \"assistant\" && typeof msg.content === \"string\") {\n        return {\n          ...msg,\n          providerOptions: {\n            ...msg.providerOptions,\n            [key]: {\n              ...msg.providerOptions?.[key],\n              [field]: \"\",\n            },\n          },\n        }\n      }\n\n      return msg\n    })\n  }\n\n  return msgs\n}\n\nfunction applyCaching(msgs: ModelMessage[], model: Provider.Model): ModelMessage[] {\n  const system = msgs.filter((msg) => msg.role === \"system\").slice(0, 2)\n  const final = msgs.filter((msg) => msg.role !== \"system\").slice(-2)\n\n  const key = providerOptionsKey(model)\n  const providerOptions = {\n    anthropic: {\n      cacheControl: { type: \"ephemeral\" },\n    },\n    openrouter: {\n      cacheControl: { type: \"ephemeral\" },\n    },\n    bedrock: {\n      cachePoint: { type: \"default\" },\n    },\n    [key]: {\n      cache_control: { type: \"ephemeral\" },\n    },\n    copilot: {\n      copilot_cache_control: { type: \"ephemeral\" },\n    },\n    alibaba: {\n      cacheControl: { type: \"ephemeral\" },\n    },\n  }\n\n  for (const msg of unique([...system, ...final])) {\n    const useMessageLevelOptions =\n      model.providerID === \"anthropic\" ||\n      model.providerID.includes(\"bedrock\") ||\n      model.api.npm === \"@ai-sdk/amazon-bedrock\"\n    const shouldUseContentOptions = !useMessageLevelOptions && Array.isArray(msg.content) && msg.content.length > 0\n\n    if (shouldUseContentOptions) {\n      const lastContent = msg.content[msg.content.length - 1]\n      if (\n        lastContent &&\n        typeof lastContent === \"object\" &&\n        lastContent.type !== \"tool-approval-request\" &&\n        lastContent.type !== \"tool-approval-response\"\n      ) {\n        lastContent.providerOptions = mergeDeep(lastContent.providerOptions ?? {}, providerOptions)\n        continue\n      }\n    }\n\n    msg.providerOptions = mergeDeep(msg.providerOptions ?? {}, providerOptions)\n  }\n\n  return msgs\n}\n\nfunction unsupportedParts(msgs: ModelMessage[], model: Provider.Model): ModelMessage[] {\n  return msgs.map((msg) => {\n    if (msg.role !== \"user\" || !Array.isArray(msg.content)) return msg\n\n    const filtered = msg.content.map((part) => {\n      if (part.type !== \"file\" && part.type !== \"image\") return part\n\n      // Check for empty base64 image data\n      if (part.type === \"image\") {\n        const imageStr = String(part.image)\n        if (imageStr.startsWith(\"data:\")) {\n          const match = imageStr.match(/^data:([^;]+);base64,(.*)$/)\n          if (match && (!match[2] || match[2].length === 0)) {\n            return {\n              type: \"text\" as const,\n              text: \"ERROR: Image file is empty or corrupted. Please provide a valid image.\",\n            }\n          }\n        }\n      }\n\n      const mime = part.type === \"image\" ? String(part.image).split(\";\")[0].replace(\"data:\", \"\") : part.mediaType\n      const filename = part.type === \"file\" ? part.filename : undefined\n      const modality = mimeToModality(mime)\n      if (!modality) return part\n      if (model.capabilities.input[modality]) return part\n\n      const name = filename ? `\"${filename}\"` : modality\n      return {\n        type: \"text\" as const,\n        text: `ERROR: Cannot read ${name} (this model does not support ${modality} input). Inform the user.`,\n      }\n    })\n\n    return { ...msg, content: filtered }\n  })\n}\n\nexport function message(msgs: ModelMessage[], model: Provider.Model, options: Record<string, unknown>) {\n  msgs = unsupportedParts(msgs, model)\n  msgs = normalizeMessages(msgs, model, options)\n  if (\n    (model.providerID === \"anthropic\" ||\n      model.providerID === \"google-vertex-anthropic\" ||\n      model.api.id.includes(\"anthropic\") ||\n      model.api.id.includes(\"claude\") ||\n      model.id.includes(\"anthropic\") ||\n      model.id.includes(\"claude\") ||\n      model.api.npm === \"@ai-sdk/anthropic\" ||\n      model.api.npm === \"@ai-sdk/alibaba\") &&\n    model.api.npm !== \"@ai-sdk/gateway\"\n  ) {\n    msgs = applyCaching(msgs, model)\n  }\n\n  // Remap providerOptions keys from stored providerID to expected SDK key\n  const key = sdkKey(model.api.npm)\n  if (key && key !== model.providerID) {\n    const remap = (opts: Record<string, any> | undefined) => {\n      if (!opts) return opts\n      if (!(model.providerID in opts)) return opts\n      const result = { ...opts }\n      result[key] = result[model.providerID]\n      delete result[model.providerID]\n      return result\n    }\n\n    msgs = msgs.map((msg) => {\n      if (!Array.isArray(msg.content)) return { ...msg, providerOptions: remap(msg.providerOptions) }\n      return {\n        ...msg,\n        providerOptions: remap(msg.providerOptions),\n        content: msg.content.map((part) => {\n          if (part.type === \"tool-approval-request\" || part.type === \"tool-approval-response\") {\n            return { ...part }\n          }\n          return { ...part, providerOptions: remap(part.providerOptions) }\n        }),\n      } as typeof msg\n    })\n  }\n\n  return msgs\n}\n\nexport function temperature(model: Provider.Model) {\n  const id = model.id.toLowerCase()\n  if (id.includes(\"qwen\")) return 0.55\n  if (id.includes(\"claude\")) return undefined\n  if (id.includes(\"gemini\")) return 1.0\n  if (id.includes(\"glm-4.6\")) return 1.0\n  if (id.includes(\"glm-4.7\")) return 1.0\n  if (id.includes(\"minimax-m2\")) return 1.0\n  if (id.includes(\"kimi-k2\")) {\n    // kimi-k2-thinking & kimi-k2.5 && kimi-k2p5 && kimi-k2-5\n    if ([\"thinking\", \"k2.\", \"k2p\", \"k2-5\"].some((s) => id.includes(s))) {\n      return 1.0\n    }\n    return 0.6\n  }\n  return undefined\n}\n\nexport function topP(model: Provider.Model) {\n  const id = model.id.toLowerCase()\n  if (id.includes(\"qwen\")) return 1\n  if ([\"minimax-m2\", \"gemini\", \"kimi-k2.5\", \"kimi-k2p5\", \"kimi-k2-5\"].some((s) => id.includes(s))) {\n    return 0.95\n  }\n  return undefined\n}\n\nexport function topK(model: Provider.Model) {\n  const id = model.id.toLowerCase()\n  if (id.includes(\"minimax-m2\")) {\n    if ([\"m2.\", \"m25\", \"m21\"].some((s) => id.includes(s))) return 40\n    return 20\n  }\n  if (id.includes(\"gemini\")) return 64\n  return undefined\n}\n\nconst WIDELY_SUPPORTED_EFFORTS = [\"low\", \"medium\", \"high\"]\nconst OPENAI_EFFORTS = [\"none\", \"minimal\", ...WIDELY_SUPPORTED_EFFORTS, \"xhigh\"]\n\nfunction anthropicAdaptiveEfforts(apiId: string): string[] | null {\n  if ([\"opus-4-7\", \"opus-4.7\"].some((v) => apiId.includes(v))) {\n    return [\"low\", \"medium\", \"high\", \"xhigh\", \"max\"]\n  }\n  if ([\"opus-4-6\", \"opus-4.6\", \"sonnet-4-6\", \"sonnet-4.6\"].some((v) => apiId.includes(v))) {\n    return [\"low\", \"medium\", \"high\", \"max\"]\n  }\n  return null\n}\n\nexport function variants(model: Provider.Model): Record<string, Record<string, any>> {\n  if (!model.capabilities.reasoning) return {}\n\n  const id = model.id.toLowerCase()\n  const adaptiveEfforts = anthropicAdaptiveEfforts(model.api.id)\n  if (\n    id.includes(\"deepseek\") ||\n    id.includes(\"minimax\") ||\n    id.includes(\"glm\") ||\n    id.includes(\"kimi\") ||\n    id.includes(\"k2p\") ||\n    id.includes(\"qwen\") ||\n    id.includes(\"big-pickle\")\n  )\n    return {}\n\n  // see: https://docs.x.ai/docs/guides/reasoning#control-how-hard-the-model-thinks\n  if (id.includes(\"grok\") && id.includes(\"grok-3-mini\")) {\n    if (model.api.npm === \"@openrouter/ai-sdk-provider\") {\n      return {\n        low: { reasoning: { effort: \"low\" } },\n        high: { reasoning: { effort: \"high\" } },\n      }\n    }\n    return {\n      low: { reasoningEffort: \"low\" },\n      high: { reasoningEffort: \"high\" },\n    }\n  }\n  if (id.includes(\"grok\")) return {}\n\n  switch (model.api.npm) {\n    case \"@openrouter/ai-sdk-provider\":\n      if (!model.id.includes(\"gpt\") && !model.id.includes(\"gemini-3\") && !model.id.includes(\"claude\")) return {}\n      return Object.fromEntries(OPENAI_EFFORTS.map((effort) => [effort, { reasoning: { effort } }]))\n\n    case \"@ai-sdk/gateway\":\n      if (model.id.includes(\"anthropic\")) {\n        if (adaptiveEfforts) {\n          return Object.fromEntries(\n            adaptiveEfforts.map((effort) => [\n              effort,\n              {\n                thinking: {\n                  type: \"adaptive\",\n                },\n                effort,\n              },\n            ]),\n          )\n        }\n        return {\n          high: {\n            thinking: {\n              type: \"enabled\",\n              budgetTokens: 16000,\n            },\n          },\n          max: {\n            thinking: {\n              type: \"enabled\",\n              budgetTokens: 31999,\n            },\n          },\n        }\n      }\n      if (model.id.includes(\"google\")) {\n        if (id.includes(\"2.5\")) {\n          return {\n            high: {\n              thinkingConfig: {\n                includeThoughts: true,\n                thinkingBudget: 16000,\n              },\n            },\n            max: {\n              thinkingConfig: {\n                includeThoughts: true,\n                thinkingBudget: 24576,\n              },\n            },\n          }\n        }\n        return Object.fromEntries(\n          [\"low\", \"high\"].map((effort) => [\n            effort,\n            {\n              includeThoughts: true,\n              thinkingLevel: effort,\n            },\n          ]),\n        )\n      }\n      return Object.fromEntries(OPENAI_EFFORTS.map((effort) => [effort, { reasoningEffort: effort }]))\n\n    case \"@ai-sdk/github-copilot\":\n      if (model.id.includes(\"gemini\")) {\n        // currently github copilot only returns thinking\n        return {}\n      }\n      if (model.id.includes(\"claude\")) {\n        return Object.fromEntries(WIDELY_SUPPORTED_EFFORTS.map((effort) => [effort, { reasoningEffort: effort }]))\n      }\n      const copilotEfforts = iife(() => {\n        if (id.includes(\"5.1-codex-max\") || id.includes(\"5.2\") || id.includes(\"5.3\"))\n          return [...WIDELY_SUPPORTED_EFFORTS, \"xhigh\"]\n        const arr = [...WIDELY_SUPPORTED_EFFORTS]\n        if (id.includes(\"gpt-5\") && model.release_date >= \"2025-12-04\") arr.push(\"xhigh\")\n        return arr\n      })\n      return Object.fromEntries(\n        copilotEfforts.map((effort) => [\n          effort,\n          {\n            reasoningEffort: effort,\n            reasoningSummary: \"auto\",\n            include: [\"reasoning.encrypted_content\"],\n          },\n        ]),\n      )\n\n    case \"@ai-sdk/cerebras\":\n    // https://v5.ai-sdk.dev/providers/ai-sdk-providers/cerebras\n    case \"@ai-sdk/togetherai\":\n    // https://v5.ai-sdk.dev/providers/ai-sdk-providers/togetherai\n    case \"@ai-sdk/xai\":\n    // https://v5.ai-sdk.dev/providers/ai-sdk-providers/xai\n    case \"@ai-sdk/deepinfra\":\n    // https://v5.ai-sdk.dev/providers/ai-sdk-providers/deepinfra\n    case \"venice-ai-sdk-provider\":\n    // https://docs.venice.ai/overview/guides/reasoning-models#reasoning-effort\n    case \"@ai-sdk/openai-compatible\":\n      return Object.fromEntries(WIDELY_SUPPORTED_EFFORTS.map((effort) => [effort, { reasoningEffort: effort }]))\n\n    case \"@ai-sdk/azure\":\n      // https://v5.ai-sdk.dev/providers/ai-sdk-providers/azure\n      if (id === \"o1-mini\") return {}\n      const azureEfforts = [\"low\", \"medium\", \"high\"]\n      if (id.includes(\"gpt-5-\") || id === \"gpt-5\") {\n        azureEfforts.unshift(\"minimal\")\n      }\n      return Object.fromEntries(\n        azureEfforts.map((effort) => [\n          effort,\n          {\n            reasoningEffort: effort,\n            reasoningSummary: \"auto\",\n            include: [\"reasoning.encrypted_content\"],\n          },\n        ]),\n      )\n    case \"@ai-sdk/openai\":\n      // https://v5.ai-sdk.dev/providers/ai-sdk-providers/openai\n      if (id === \"gpt-5-pro\") return {}\n      const openaiEfforts = iife(() => {\n        if (id.includes(\"codex\")) {\n          if (id.includes(\"5.2\") || id.includes(\"5.3\")) return [...WIDELY_SUPPORTED_EFFORTS, \"xhigh\"]\n          return WIDELY_SUPPORTED_EFFORTS\n        }\n        const arr = [...WIDELY_SUPPORTED_EFFORTS]\n        if (id.includes(\"gpt-5-\") || id === \"gpt-5\") {\n          arr.unshift(\"minimal\")\n        }\n        if (model.release_date >= \"2025-11-13\") {\n          arr.unshift(\"none\")\n        }\n        if (model.release_date >= \"2025-12-04\") {\n          arr.push(\"xhigh\")\n        }\n        return arr\n      })\n      return Object.fromEntries(\n        openaiEfforts.map((effort) => [\n          effort,\n          {\n            reasoningEffort: effort,\n            reasoningSummary: \"auto\",\n            include: [\"reasoning.encrypted_content\"],\n          },\n        ]),\n      )\n\n    case \"@ai-sdk/anthropic\":\n    // https://v5.ai-sdk.dev/providers/ai-sdk-providers/anthropic\n    case \"@ai-sdk/google-vertex/anthropic\":\n      // https://v5.ai-sdk.dev/providers/ai-sdk-providers/google-vertex#anthropic-provider\n\n      if (model.providerID === \"github-copilot\") {\n        if (model.api.id.includes(\"opus-4.7\")) {\n          return Object.fromEntries([\"medium\"].map((effort) => [effort, { reasoningEffort: effort }]))\n        }\n      }\n\n      if (adaptiveEfforts) {\n        return Object.fromEntries(\n          adaptiveEfforts.map((effort) => [\n            effort,\n            {\n              thinking: {\n                type: \"adaptive\",\n                ...(model.api.id.includes(\"opus-4-7\") || model.api.id.includes(\"opus-4.7\")\n                  ? { display: \"summarized\" }\n                  : {}),\n              },\n              effort,\n            },\n          ]),\n        )\n      }\n\n      return {\n        high: {\n          thinking: {\n            type: \"enabled\",\n            budgetTokens: Math.min(16_000, Math.floor(model.limit.output / 2 - 1)),\n          },\n        },\n        max: {\n          thinking: {\n            type: \"enabled\",\n            budgetTokens: Math.min(31_999, model.limit.output - 1),\n          },\n        },\n      }\n\n    case \"@ai-sdk/amazon-bedrock\":\n      // https://v5.ai-sdk.dev/providers/ai-sdk-providers/amazon-bedrock\n      if (adaptiveEfforts) {\n        return Object.fromEntries(\n          adaptiveEfforts.map((effort) => [\n            effort,\n            {\n              reasoningConfig: {\n                type: \"adaptive\",\n                maxReasoningEffort: effort,\n                ...(model.api.id.includes(\"opus-4-7\") || model.api.id.includes(\"opus-4.7\")\n                  ? { display: \"summarized\" }\n                  : {}),\n              },\n            },\n          ]),\n        )\n      }\n      // For Anthropic models on Bedrock, use reasoningConfig with budgetTokens\n      if (model.api.id.includes(\"anthropic\")) {\n        return {\n          high: {\n Provider.Model\n  sessionID: string\n  providerOptions?: Record<string, any>\n}): Record<string, any> {\n  const result: Record<string, any> = {}\n\n  // openai and providers using openai package (toolCall.hasFinished) {\n                  continue\n                }\n\n                if (toolCallDelta.function?.arguments != null) {\n                  toolCall.function!.arguments +=
