 type: \"unsupported\",\n          feature: \"reasoningEffort\",\n          details: \"reasoningEffort is not supported for non-reasoning models\",\n        })\n      }\n\n      if (openaiOptions?.reasoningSummary != null) {\n        warnings.push({\n          type: \"unsupported\",\n          feature: \"reasoningSummary\",\n          details: \"reasoningSummary is not supported for non-reasoning models\",\n        })\n      }\n    }\n\n    // Validate flex processing support\n    if (openaiOptions?.serviceTier === \"flex\" && !modelConfig.supportsFlexProcessing) {\n      warnings.push({\n        type: \"unsupported\",\n        feature: \"serviceTier\",\n        details: \"flex processing is only available for o3, o4-mini, and gpt-5 models\",\n      })\n      // Remove from args if not supported\n      baseArgs.service_tier = undefined\n    }\n\n    // Validate priority processing support\n    if (openaiOptions?.serviceTier === \"priority\" && !modelConfig.supportsPriorityProcessing) {\n      warnings.push({\n        type: \"unsupported\",\n        feature: \"serviceTier\",\n        details:\n          \"priority processing is only available for supported models (gpt-4, gpt-5, gpt-5-mini, o3, o4-mini) and requires Enterprise access. gpt-5-nano is not supported\",\n      })\n      // Remove from args if not supported\n      baseArgs.service_tier = undefined\n    }\n\n    const {\n      tools: openaiTools,\n      toolChoice: openaiToolChoice,\n      toolWarnings,\n    } = prepareResponsesTools({\n      tools,\n      toolChoice,\n      strictJsonSchema,\n    })\n\n    return {\n      webSearchToolName,\n      args: {\n        ...baseArgs,\n        tools: openaiTools,\n        tool_choice: openaiToolChoice,\n      },\n      warnings: [...warnings, ...toolWarnings],\n    }\n  }\n\n  async doGenerate(options: LanguageModelV3CallOptions) {\n    const { args: body, warnings, webSearchToolName } = await this.getArgs(options)\n    const url = this.config.url({\n      path: \"/responses\",\n      modelId: this.modelId,\n    })\n\n    const {\n      responseHeaders,\n      value: response,\n      rawValue: rawResponse,\n    } = await postJsonToApi({\n      url,\n      headers: combineHeaders(this.config.headers(), options.headers),\n      body,\n      failedResponseHandler: openaiFailedResponseHandler,\n      successfulResponseHandler: createJsonResponseHandler(\n        z.object({\n          id: z.string(),\n          created_at: z.number(),\n          error: z\n            .object({\n              code: z.string(),\n              message: z.string(),\n            })\n            .nullish(),\n          model: z.string(),\n          output: z.array(\n            z.discriminatedUnion(\"type\", [\n              z.object({\n                type: z.literal(\"message\"),\n                role: z.literal(\"assistant\"),\n                id: z.string(),\n                content: z.array(\n                  z.object({\n                    type: z.literal(\"output_text\"),\n                    text: z.string(),\n                    logprobs: LOGPROBS_SCHEMA.nullish(),\n                    annotations: z.array(\n                      z.discriminatedUnion(\"type\", [\n                        z.object({\n                          type: z.literal(\"url_citation\"),\n                          start_index: z.number(),\n                          end_index: z.number(),\n                          url: z.string(),\n                          title: z.string(),\n                        }),\n                        z.object({\n                          type: z.literal(\"file_citation\"),\n                          file_id: z.string(),\n                          filename: z.string().nullish(),\n                          index: z.number().nullish(),\n                          start_index: z.number().nullish(),\n                          end_index: z.number().nullish(),\n                          quote: z.string().nullish(),\n                        }),\n                        z.object({\n                          type: z.literal(\"container_file_citation\"),\n                        }),\n                      ]),\n                    ),\n                  }),\n                ),\n              }),\n              webSearchCallItem,\n              fileSearchCallItem,\n              codeInterpreterCallItem,\n              imageGenerationCallItem,\n              localShellCallItem,\n              z.object({\n                type: z.literal(\"function_call\"),\n                call_id: z.string(),\n                name: z.string(),\n                arguments: z.string(),\n                id: z.string(),\n              }),\n              z.object({\n                type: z.literal(\"computer_call\"),\n                id: z.string(),\n                status: z.string().optional(),\n              }),\n              z.object({\n                type: z.literal(\"reasoning\"),\n                id: z.string(),\n                encrypted_content: z.string().nullish(),\n                summary: z.array(\n                  z.object({\n                    type: z.literal(\"summary_text\"),\n                    text: z.string(),\n                  }),\n                ),\n              }),\n            ]),\n          ),\n          service_tier: z.string().nullish(),\n          incomplete_details: z.object({ reason: z.string() }).nullish(),\n          usage: usageSchema,\n        }),\n      ),\n      abortSignal: options.abortSignal,\n      fetch: this.config.fetch,\n    })\n\n    if (response.error) {\n      throw new APICallError({\n        message: response.error.message,\n        url,\n        requestBodyValues: body,\n        statusCode: 400,\n        responseHeaders,\n        responseBody: rawResponse as string,\n        isRetryable: false,\n      })\n    }\n\n    const content: Array<LanguageModelV3Content> = []\n    const logprobs: Array<z.infer<typeof LOGPROBS_SCHEMA>> = []\n\n    // flag that checks if there have been client-side tool calls (not executed by openai)\n    let hasFunctionCall = false\n\n    // map response content to content array\n    for (const part of response.output) {\n      switch (part.type) {\n        case \"reasoning\": {\n          // when there are no summary parts, we need to add an empty reasoning part:\n          if (part.summary.length === 0) {\n            part.summary.push({ type: \"summary_text\", text: \"\" })\n          }\n\n          for (const summary of part.summary) {\n            content.push({\n              type: \"reasoning\" as const,\n              text: summary.text,\n              providerMetadata: {\n                openai: {\n                  itemId: part.id,\n                  reasoningEncryptedContent: part.encrypted_content ?? null,\n                },\n              },\n            })\n          }\n          break\n        }\n\n        case \"image_generation_call\": {\n          content.push({\n            type: \"tool-call\",\n            toolCallId: part.id,\n            toolName: \"image_generation\",\n            input: \"{}\",\n            providerExecuted: true,\n          })\n\n          content.push({\n            type: \"tool-result\",\n            toolCallId: part.id,\n            toolName: \"image_generation\",\n            result: {\n              result: part.result,\n            } satisfies z.infer<typeof imageGenerationOutputSchema>,\n          })\n\n          break\n        }\n\n        case \"local_shell_call\": {\n          content.push({\n            type: \"tool-call\",\n            toolCallId: part.call_id,\n            toolName: \"local_shell\",\n            input: JSON.stringify({ action: part.action } satisfies z.infer<typeof localShellInputSchema>),\n            providerMetadata: {\n              openai: {\n                itemId: part.id,\n              },\n            },\n          })\n\n          break\n        }\n\n        case \"message\": {\n          for (const contentPart of part.content) {\n            if (options.providerOptions?.openai?.logprobs && contentPart.logprobs) {\n              logprobs.push(contentPart.logprobs)\n            }\n\n            content.push({\n              type: \"text\",\n              text: contentPart.text,\n              providerMetadata: {\n                openai: {\n                  itemId: part.id,\n                },\n              },\n            })\n\n            for (const annotation of contentPart.annotations) {\n              if (annotation.type === \"url_citation\") {\n                content.push({\n                  type: \"source\",\n                  sourceType: \"url\",\n                  id: this.config.generateId?.() ?? generateId(),\n                  url: annotation.url,\n                  title: annotation.title,\n                })\n              } else if (annotation.type === \"file_citation\") {\n                content.push({\n                  type: \"source\",\n                  sourceType: \"document\",\n                  id: this.config.generateId?.() ?? generateId(),\n                  mediaType: \"text/plain\",\n                  title: annotation.quote ?? annotation.filename ?? \"Document\",\n                  filename: annotation.filename ?? annotation.file_id,\n                })\n              }\n            }\n          }\n\n          break\n        }\n\n        case \"function_call\": {\n          hasFunctionCall = true\n\n          content.push({\n            type: \"tool-call\",\n            toolCallId: part.call_id,\n            toolName: part.name,\n            input: part.arguments,\n            providerMetadata: {\n              openai: {\n                itemId: part.id,\n              },\n            },\n          })\n          break\n        }\n\n        case \"web_search_call\": {\n          content.push({\n            type: \"tool-call\",\n            toolCallId: part.id,\n            toolName: webSearchToolName ?? \"web_search\",\n            input: JSON.stringify({ action: part.action }),\n            providerExecuted: true,\n          })\n\n          content.push({\n            type: \"tool-result\",\n            toolCallId: part.id,\n            toolName: webSearchToolName ?? \"web_search\",\n            result: { status: part.status },\n          })\n\n          break\n        }\n\n        case \"computer_call\": {\n          content.push({\n            type: \"tool-call\",\n            toolCallId: part.id,\n            toolName: \"computer_use\",\n            input: \"\",\n            providerExecuted: true,\n          })\n\n          content.push({\n            type: \"tool-result\",\n            toolCallId: part.id,\n            toolName: \"computer_use\",\n            result: {\n              type: \"computer_use_tool_result\",\n              status: part.status || \"completed\",\n            },\n          })\n          break\n        }\n\n        case \"file_search_call\": {\n          content.push({\n            type: \"tool-call\",\n            toolCallId: part.id,\n            toolName: \"file_search\",\n            input: \"{}\",\n            providerExecuted: true,\n          })\n\n          content.push({\n            type: \"tool-result\",\n            toolCallId: part.id,\n            toolName: \"file_search\",\n            result: {\n              queries: part.queries,\n              results:\n                part.results?.map((result) => ({\n                  attributes: result.attributes as Record<string, JSONValue>,\n                  fileId: result.file_id,\n                  filename: result.filename,\n                  score: result.score,\n                  text: result.text,\n                })) ?? null,\n            } satisfies z.infer<typeof fileSearchOutputSchema>,\n          })\n          break\n        }\n\n        case \"code_interpreter_call\": {\n          content.push({\n            type: \"tool-call\",\n            toolCallId: part.id,\n            toolName: \"code_interpreter\",\n            input: JSON.stringify({\n              code: part.code,\n              containerId: part.container_id,\n            } satisfies z.infer<typeof codeInterpreterInputSchema>),\n            providerExecuted: true,\n          })\n\n          content.push({\n            type: \"tool-result\",\n            toolCallId: part.id,\n            toolName: \"code_interpreter\",\n            result: {\n              outputs: part.outputs,\n            } satisfies z.infer<typeof codeInterpreterOutputSchema>,\n          })\n          break\n        }\n      }\n    }\n\n    const providerMetadata: SharedV3ProviderMetadata = {\n      openai: { responseId: response.id },\n    }\n\n    if (logprobs.length > 0) {\n      providerMetadata.openai.logprobs = logprobs\n    }\n\n    if (typeof response.service_tier === \"string\") {\n      providerMetadata.openai.serviceTier = response.service_tier\n    }\n\n    return {\n      content,\n      finishReason: {\n        unified: mapOpenAIResponseFinishReason({\n          finishReason: response.incomplete_details?.reason,\n          hasFunctionCall,\n        }),\n        raw: response.incomplete_details?.reason,\n      },\n      usage: {\n        inputTokens: {\n          total: response.usage.input_tokens,\n          noCache:\n            response.usage.input_tokens_details?.cached_tokens != null\n              ? response.usage.input_tokens - response.usage.input_tokens_details.cached_tokens\n              : undefined,\n          cacheRead: response.usage.input_tokens_details?.cached_tokens ?? undefined,\n          cacheWrite: undefined,\n        },\n        outputTokens: {\n          total: response.usage.output_tokens,\n          text: undefined,\n          reasoning: response.usage.output_tokens_details?.reasoning_tokens ?? undefined,\n        },\n        raw: response.usage,\n      },\n      request: { body },\n      response: {\n        id: response.id,\n        timestamp: new Date(response.created_at * 1000),\n        modelId: response.model,\n        headers: responseHeaders,\n        body: rawResponse,\n      },\n      providerMetadata,\n      warnings,\n    }\n  }\n\n  async doStream(options: LanguageModelV3CallOptions) {\n    const { args: body, warnings, webSearchToolName } = await this.getArgs(options)\n\n    const { responseHeaders, value: response } = await postJsonToApi({\n      url: this.config.url({\n        path: \"/responses\",\n        modelId: this.modelId,\n      }),\n      headers: combineHeaders(this.config.headers(), options.headers),\n      body: {\n        ...body,\n        stream: true,\n      },\n      failedResponseHandler: openaiFailedResponseHandler,\n      successfulResponseHandler: createEventSourceResponseHandler(openaiResponsesChunkSchema),\n      abortSignal: options.abortSignal,\n      fetch: this.config.fetch,\n    })\n\n    // oxlint-disable-next-line no-this-alias -- needed for closure scope inside generator\n    const self = this\n\n    let finishReason: {\n      unified: ReturnType<typeof mapOpenAIResponseFinishReason>\n      raw: string | undefined\n    } = {\n      unified: \"other\",\n      raw: undefined,\n    }\n    const usage: {\n      inputTokens: number | undefined\n      outputTokens: number | undefined\n      totalTokens: number | undefined\n      reasoningTokens: number | undefined\n      cachedInputTokens: number | undefined\n    } = {\n      inputTokens: undefined,\n      outputTokens: undefined,\n      totalTokens: undefined,\n      reasoningTokens: undefined,\n      cachedInputTokens: undefined,\n    }\n    const logprobs: Array<z.infer<typeof LOGPROBS_SCHEMA>> = []\n    let responseId: string | null = null\n    const ongoingToolCalls: Record<\n      number,\n      | {\n          toolName: string\n          toolCallId: string\n          codeInterpreter?: {\n            containerId: string\n          }\n        }\n      | undefined\n    > = {}\n\n    // flag that checks if there have been client-side tool calls (not executed by openai)\n    let hasFunctionCall = false\n\n    // Track reasoning by output_index instead of item_id\n    // GitHub Copilot rotates encrypted item IDs on every event\n    const activeReasoning: Record<\n      number,\n      {\n        canonicalId: string // the item.id from output_item.added\n        encryptedContent?: string | null\n        summaryParts: number[]\n      }\n    > = {}\n\n    // Track current active reasoning output_index for correlating summary events\n    let currentReasoningOutputIndex: number | null = null\n\n    // Track a stable text part id for the current assistant message.\n    // Copilot may change item_id across text deltas; normalize to one id.\n    let currentTextId: string | null = null\n\n    let serviceTier: string | undefined\n\n    return {\n      stream: response.pipeThrough(\n        new TransformStream<ParseResult<z.infer<typeof openaiResponsesChunkSchema>>, LanguageModelV3StreamPart>({\n          start(controller) {\n            controller.enqueue({ type: \"stream-start\", warnings })\n          },\n\n          transform(chunk, controller) {\n            if (options.includeRawChunks) {\n              controller.enqueue({ type: \"raw\", rawValue: chunk.rawValue })\n            }\n\n            // handle failed chunk parsing / validation:\n            if (!chunk.success) {\n              finishReason = {\n                unified: \"error\",\n                raw: undefined,\n              }\n              controller.enqueue({ type: \"error\", error: chunk.error })\n              return\n            }\n\n            const value = chunk.value\n\n            if (isResponseOutputItemAddedChunk(value)) {\n              if (value.item.type === \"function_call\") {\n                ongoingToolCalls[value.output_index] = {\n                  toolName: value.item.name,\n                  toolCallId: value.item.call_id,\n                }\n\n                controller.enqueue({\n                  type: \"tool-input-start\",\n                  id: value.item.call_id,\n                  toolName: value.item.name,\n                })\n              } else if (value.item.type === \"web_search_call\") {\n                ongoingToolCalls[value.output_index] = {\n                  toolName: webSearchToolName ?? \"web_search\",\n                  toolCallId: value.item.id,\n                }\n\n                controller.enqueue({\n                  type: \"tool-input-start\",\n                  id: value.item.id,\n                  toolName: webSearchToolName ?? \"web_search\",\n                })\n              } else if (value.item.type === \"computer_call\") {\n                ongoingToolCalls[value.output_index] = {\n                  toolName: \"computer_use\",\n                  toolCallId: value.item.id,\n                }\n\n                controller.enqueue({\n                  type: \"tool-input-start\",\n                  id: value.item.id,\n                  toolName: \"computer_use\",\n                })\n              } else if (value.item.type === \"code_interpreter_call\") {\n                ongoingToolCalls[value.output_index] = {\n                  toolName: \"code_interpreter\",\n                  toolCallId: value.item.id,\n                  codeInterpreter: {\n                    containerId: value.item.container_id,\n                  },\n                }\n\n                controller.enqueue({\n                  type: \"tool-input-start\",\n                  id: value.item.id,\n                  toolName: \"code_interpreter\",\n                })\n\n                controller.enqueue({\n                  type: \"tool-input-delta\",\n                  id: value.item.id,\n                  delta: `{\"containerId\":\"${value.item.container_id}\",\"code\":\"`,\n                })\n              } else if (value.item.type === \"file_search_call\") {\n                controller.enqueue({\n                  type: \"tool-call\",\n                  toolCallId: value.item.id,\n                  toolName: \"file_search\",\n                  input: \"{}\",\n                  providerExecuted: true,\n                })\n              } else if (value.item.type === \"image_generation_call\") {\n                controller.enqueue({\n                  type: \"tool-call\",\n                  toolCallId: value.item.id,\n                  toolName: \"image_generation\",\n                  input: \"{}\",\n                  providerExecuted: true,\n                })\n              } else if (value.item.type === \"message\") {\n                // Start a stable text part for this assistant message\n                currentTextId = value.item.id\n                controller.enqueue({\n                  type: \"text-start\",\n                  id: value.item.id,\n                  providerMetadata: {\n                    openai: {\n                      itemId: value.item.id,\n                    },\n                  },\n                })\n              } else if (isResponseOutputItemAddedReasoningChunk(value)) {\n                activeReasoning[value.output_index] = {\n                  canonicalId: value.item.id,\n                  encryptedContent: value.item.encrypted_content,\n                  summaryParts: [0],\n                }\n                currentReasoningOutputIndex = value.output_index\n\n                controller.enqueue({\n                  type: \"reasoning-start\",\n                  id: `${value.item.id}:0`,\n                  providerMetadata: {\n                    openai: {\n                      itemId: value.item.id,\n                      reasoningEncryptedContent: value.item.encrypted_content ?? null,\n                    },\n                  },\n                })\n              }\n            } else if (isResponseOutputItemDoneChunk(value)) {\n              if (value.item.type === \"function_call\") {\n                ongoingToolCalls[value.output_index] = undefined\n                hasFunctionCall = true\n\n                controller.enqueue({\n                  type: \"tool-input-end\",\n                  id: value.item.call_id,\n                })\n\n                controller.enqueue({\n                  type: \"tool-call\",\n                  toolCallId: value.item.call_id,\n                  toolName: value.item.name,\n                  input: value.item.arguments,\n                  providerMetadata: {\n                    openai: {\n                      itemId: value.item.id,\n                    },\n                  },\n                })\n              } else if (value.item.type === \"web_search_call\") {\n                ongoingToolCalls[value.output_index] = undefined\n\n                controller.enqueue({\n                  type: \"tool-input-end\",\n                  id: value.item.id,\n                })\n\n                controller.enqueue({\n                  type: \"tool-call\",\n                  toolCallId: value.item.id,\n                  toolName: \"web_search\",\n                  input: JSON.stringify({ action: value.item.action }),\n                  providerExecuted: true,\n                })\n\n                controller.enqueue({\n                  type: \"tool-result\",\n                  toolCallId: value.item.id,\n                  toolName: \"web_search\",\n                  result: { status: value.item.status },\n                })\n              } else if (value.item.type === \"computer_call\") {\n                ongoingToolCalls[value.output_index] = undefined\n\n                controller.enqueue({\n                  type: \"tool-input-end\",\n                  id: value.item.id,\n                })\n\n                controller.enqueue({\n                  type: \"tool-call\",\n                  toolCallId: value.item.id,\n                  toolName: \"computer_use\",\n                  input: \"\",\n                  providerExecuted: true,\n                })\n\n                controller.enqueue({\n                  type: \"tool-result\",\n                  toolCallId: value.item.id,\n                  toolName: \"computer_use\",\n                  result: {\n                    type: \"computer_use_tool_result\",\n                    status: value.item.status || \"completed\",\n                  },\n                })\n              } else if (value.item.type === \"file_search_call\") {\n                ongoingToolCalls[value.output_index] = undefined\n\n                controller.enqueue({\n                  type: \"tool-result\",\n                  toolCallId: value.item.id,\n                  toolName: \"file_search\",\n                  result: {\n                    queries: value.item.queries,\n                    results:\n                      value.item.results?.map((result) => ({\n                        attributes: result.attributes as Record<string, JSONValue>,\n                        fileId: result.file_id,\n                        filename: result.filename,\n                        score: result.score,\n                        text: result.text,\n                      })) ?? null,\n                  } satisfies z.infer<typeof fileSearchOutputSchema>,\n                })\n              } else if (value.item.type === \"code_interpreter_call\") {\n                ongoingToolCalls[value.output_index] = undefined\n\n                controller.enqueue({\n                  type: \"tool-result\",\n                  toolCallId: value.item.id,\n                  toolName: \"code_interpreter\",\n                  result: {\n                    outputs: value.item.outputs,\n                  } satisfies z.infer<typeof codeInterpreterOutputSchema>,\n                })\n              } else if (value.item.type === \"image_generation_call\") {\n                controller.enqueue({\n                  type: \"tool-result\",\n                  toolCallId: value.item.id,\n                  toolName: \"image_generation\",\n                  result: {\n                    result: value.item.result,\n                  } satisfies z.infer<typeof imageGenerationOutputSchema>,\n                })\n              } else if (value.item.type === \"local_shell_call\") {\n                ongoingToolCalls[value.output_index] = undefined\n\n                controller.enqueue({\n                  type: \"tool-call\",\n                  toolCallId: value.item.call_id,\n                  toolName: \"local_shell\",\n                  input: JSON.stringify({\n                    action: {\n                      type: \"exec\",\n                      command: value.item.action.command,\n                      timeoutMs: value.item.action.timeout_ms,\n                      user: value.item.action.user,\n                      workingDirectory: value.item.action.working_directory,\n                      env: value.item.action.env,\n                    },\n                  } satisfies z.infer<typeof localShellInputSchema>),\n                  providerMetadata: {\n                    openai: { itemId: value.item.id },\n                  },\n                })\n              } else if (value.item.type === \"message\") {\n                if (currentTextId) {\n                  controller.enqueue({\n                    type: \"text-end\",\n                    id: currentTextId,\n                  })\n                  currentTextId = null\n                }\n              } else if (isResponseOutputItemDoneReasoningChunk(value)) {\n                const activeReasoningPart = activeReasoning[value.output_index]\n                if (activeReasoningPart) {\n                  for (const summaryIndex of activeReasoningPart.summaryParts) {\n                    controller.enqueue({\n                      type: \"reasoning-end\",\n                      id: `${activeReasoningPart.canonicalId}:${summaryIndex}`,\n                      providerMetadata: {\n                        openai: {\n                          itemId: activeReasoningPart.canonicalId,\n                          reasoningEncryptedContent: value.item.encrypted_content ?? null,\n                        },\n                      },\n                    })\n                  }\n                  delete activeReasoning[value.output_index]\n                  if (currentReasoningOutputIndex === value.output_index) {\n                    currentReasoningOutputIndex = null\n                  }\n                }\n              }\n            } else if (isResponseFunctionCallArgumentsDeltaChunk(value)) {\n              const toolCall = ongoingToolCalls[value.output_index]\n\n              if (toolCall != null) {\n                controller.enqueue({\n                  type: \"tool-input-delta\",\n                  id: toolCall.toolCallId,\n                  delta: value.delta,\n                })\n              }\n            } else if (isResponseImageGenerationCallPartialImageChunk(value)) {\n              controller.enqueue({\n                type: \"tool-result\",\n                toolCallId: value.item_id,\n                toolName: \"image_generation\",\n                result: {\n                  result: value.partial_image_b64,\n                } satisfies z.infer<typeof imageGenerationOutputSchema>,\n              })\n            } else if (isResponseCodeInterpreterCallCodeDeltaChunk(value)) {\n              const toolCall = ongoingToolCalls[value.output_index]\n\n              if (toolCall != null) {\n                controller.enqueue({\n                  type: \"tool-input-delta\",\n                  id: toolCall.toolCallId,\n                  // The delta is code, which is embedding in a JSON string.\n                  // To escape it, we use JSON.stringify and slice to remove the outer quotes.\n                  delta: JSON.stringify(value.delta).slice(1, -1),\n                })\n              }\n            } else if (isResponseCodeInterpreterCallCodeDoneChunk(value)) {\n              const toolCall = ongoingToolCalls[value.output_index]\n\n              if (toolCall != null) {\n                controller.enqueue({\n                  type: \"tool-input-delta\",\n                  id: toolCall.toolCallId,\n                  delta: '\"}',\n                })\n\n                controller.enqueue({\n                  type: \"tool-input-end\",\n                  id: toolCall.toolCallId,\n                })\n\n                // immediately send the tool call after the input end:\n                controller.enqueue({\n                  type: \"tool-call\",\n                  toolCallId: toolCall.toolCallId,\n                  toolName: \"code_interpreter\",\n                  input: JSON.stringify({\n                    code: value.code,\n                    containerId: toolCall.codeInterpreter!.containerId,\n                  } satisfies z.infer<typeof codeInterpreterInputSchema>),\n                  providerExecuted: true,\n                })\n              }\n            } else if (isResponseCreatedChunk(value)) {\n              responseId = value.response.id\n              controller.enqueue({\n                type: \"response-metadata\",\n                id: value.response.id,\n                timestamp: new Date(value.response.created_at * 1000),\n                modelId: value.response.model,\n              })\n            } else if (isTextDeltaChunk(value)) {\n              // Ensure a text-start exists, and normalize deltas to a stable id\n              if (!currentTextId) {\n                currentTextId = value.item_id\n                controller.enqueue({\n                  type: \"text-start\",\n                  id: currentTextId,\n                  providerMetadata: {\n                    openai: { itemId: value.item_id },\n                  },\n                })\n              }\n\n              controller.enqueue({\n                type: \"text-delta\",\n                id: currentTextId,\n                delta: value.delta,\n              })\n\n              if (options.providerOptions?.openai?.logprobs && value.logprobs) {\n                logprobs.push(value.logprobs)\n              }\n            } else if (isResponseReasoningSummaryPartAddedChunk(value)) {\n              const activeItem =\n                currentReasoningOutputIndex !== null ? activeReasoning[currentReasoningOutputIndex] : null\n\n              // the first reasoning start is pushed in isResponseOutputItemAddedReasoningChunk.\n              if (activeItem && value.summary_index > 0) {\n                activeItem.summaryParts.push(value.summary_index)\n\n                controller.enqueue({\n                  type: \"reasoning-start\",\n                  id: `${activeItem.canonicalId}:${value.summary_index}`,\n                  providerMetadata: {\n                    openai: {\n                      itemId: activeItem.canonicalId,\n                      reasoningEncryptedContent: activeItem.encryptedContent ?? null,\n                    },\n                  },\n                })\n              }\n            } else if (isResponseReasoningSummaryTextDeltaChunk(value)) {\n              const activeItem =\n                currentReasoningOutputIndex !== null ? activeReasoning[currentReasoningOutputIndex] : null\n\n              if (activeItem) {\n                controller.enqueue({\n                  type: \"reasoning-delta\",\n                  id: `${activeItem.canonicalId}:${value.summary_index}`,\n                  delta: value.delta,\n                  providerMetadata: {\n                    openai: {\n                      itemId: activeItem.canonicalId,\n                    },\n                  },\n                })\n              }\n            } else if (isResponseFinishedChunk(value)) {\n              finishReason = {\n                unified: mapOpenAIResponseFinishReason({\n                  finishReason: value.response.incomplete_details?.reason,\n                  hasFunctionCall,\n                }),\n                raw: value.response.incomplete_details?.reason ?? undefined,\n              }\n              usage.inputTokens = value.response.usage.input_tokens\n              usage.outputTokens = value.response.usage.output_tokens\n              usage.totalTokens = value.response.usage.input_tokens + value.response.usage.output_tokens\n              usage.reasoningTokens = value.response.usage.output_tokens_details?.reasoning_tokens ?? undefined\n              usage.cachedInputTokens = value.response.usage.input_tokens_details?.cached_tokens ?? undefined\n              if (typeof value.response.service_tier === \"string\") {\n                serviceTier = value.response.service_tier\n              }\n            } else if (isResponseAnnotationAddedChunk(value)) {\n              if (value.annotation.type === \"url_citation\") {\n                controller.enqueue({\n                  type: \"source\",\n                  sourceType: \"url\",\n                  id: self.config.generateId?.() ?? generateId(),\n                  url: value.annotation.url,\n                  title: value.annotation.title,\n                })\n              } else if (value.annotation.type === \"file_citation\") {\n                controller.enqueue({\n                  type: \"source\",\n                  sourceType: \"document\",\n                  id: self.config.generateId?.() ?? generateId(),\n                  mediaType: \"text/plain\",\n                  title: value.annotation.quote ?? value.annotation.filename ?? \"Document\",\n                  filename: value.annotation.filename ?? value.annotation.file_id,\n                })\n              }\n            } else if (isErrorChunk(value)) {\n              controller.enqueue({ type: \"error\", error: value })\n            }\n          },\n\n          flush(controller) {\n            // Close any dangling text part\n            if (currentTextId) {\n              controller.enqueue({ type: \"text-end\", id: currentTextId })\n              currentTextId = null\n            }\n\n            const providerMetadata: SharedV3ProviderMetadata = {\n              openai: {\n                responseId,\n              },\n            }\n\n            if (logprobs.length > 0) {\n              providerMetadata.openai.logprobs = logprobs\n            }\n\n            if (serviceTier !== undefined) {\n              providerMetadata.openai.serviceTier = serviceTier\n            }\n\n            controller.enqueue({\n              type: \"finish\",\n              finishReason,\n              usage: {\n                inputTokens: {\n                  total: usage.inputTokens,\n                  noCache:\n                    usage.inputTokens != null && usage.cachedInputTokens != null\n                      ? usage.inputTokens - usage.cachedInputTokens\n                      : undefined,\n                  cacheRead: usage.cachedInputTokens,\n                  cacheWrite: undefined,\n                },\n                outputTokens: {\n                  total: usage.outputTokens,\n                  text: undefined,\n                  reasoning: usage.reasoningTokens,\n                },\n                raw: {\n                  input_tokens: usage.inputTokens,\n                  output_tokens: usage.outputTokens,\n                  total_tokens: usage.totalTokens,\n                },\n              },\n              providerMetadata,\n            })\n          },\n        }),\n      ),\n      request: { body },\n      response: { headers: responseHeaders },\n    }\n  }\n}\n\nconst usageSchema = 工作区完整探索报告\n\n## 一、目录结构\n\n```\nopencode-provider/\n├── package.json                          # 根包描述（monorepo 根）\n├── tsconfig.json                         # TypeScript 编译配置\n├── README.md                             # 项目说明\n└── packages/\n    └── opencode/\n        ├── package.json                  # @opencode-ai/opencode 包\n        ├── README.md                     # 包说明\n        └── src/\n            └── provider/\n                ├── index.ts              # 模块导出入口\n                ├── provider.ts           # 核心 Provider 系统（~1000行）\n                ├── auth.ts               # 提供方认证（OAuth/API Key）\n                ├── error.ts              # API 错误解析与分类\n                ├── models.ts             # 模型数据获取与缓存\n                ├── models-snapshot.d.ts   # 构建时快照类型声明\n                ├── schema.ts             # ProviderID/ModelID 品牌类型\n                ├── transform.ts          # 消息转换、推理配置、工具准备\n                └── sdk/\n                    └── copilot/\n                        ├── index.ts                          # 导出入口\n                        ├── copilot-provider.ts               # OpenAI 兼容 Provider 工厂\n                        ├── openai-compatible-error.ts        # 错误 Schema 定义\n                        ├── README.md                         # 说明（仅用于 Copilot）\n                        ├── chat/\n                        │   ├── openai-compatible-chat-language-model.ts  # Chat 模型实现\n                        │   ├── openai-compatible-chat-options.ts         # Chat 选项 Schema\n                        │   ├── openai-compatible-api-types.ts            # Chat API 类型定义\n                        │   ├── convert-to-openai-compatible-chat-messages.ts  # 消息转换\n                        │   ├── get-response-metadata.ts                  # 响应元数据提取\n                        │   ├── map-openai-compatible-finish-reason.ts    # 结束原因映射\n                        │   ├── openai-compatible-metadata-extractor.ts   # 元数据提取器接口\n                        │   └── openai-compatible-prepare-tools.ts        # 工具准备\n                        └── responses/\n                            ├── openai-responses-language-model.ts  # Responses API 模型实现\n                            ├── openai-responses-api-types.ts      # Responses API 类型定义\n                            ├── openai-config.ts                   # 配置接口\n                            ├── openai-error.ts                    # 错误处理\n                            ├── openai-responses-prepare-tools.ts  # 工具准备\n                            ├── openai-responses-settings.ts       # 模型 ID 类型\n                            ├── convert-to-openai-responses-input.ts   # 输入转换\n                            ├── map-openai-responses-finish-reason.ts  # 结束原因映射\n                            └── tool/\n                                ├── code-interpreter.ts    # 代码解释器工具\n                                ├── file-search.ts         # 文件搜索工具\n                                ├── image-generation.ts    # 图像生成工具\n                                ├── local-shell.ts         # 本地 Shell 工具\n                                ├── web-search-preview.ts  # 网页搜索预览工具\n                                └── web-search.ts          # 网页搜索工具\n```\n\n---\n\n## 二、每个文件的核心功能与关键逻辑\n\n### 1. 根目录文件\n\n| 文件 | 核心功能 |\n|------|---------|\n| `package.json` | monorepo 根，包名 `opencode-provider`，私有项目，用于实验复现 |\n| `tsconfig.json` | TypeScript 配置：`ESNext` 目标 + `ESNext` 模块 + 严格模式 |\n| `README.md` | 说明这是 opencode Provider 系统的最小源码，用于工具调用推理语言漂移实验 |\n\n---\n\n### 2. `packages/opencode/src/provider/index.ts`\n**核心功能**：模块导出入口。将以下子模块统一导出为命名空间：\n- `Provider` → `./provider`\n- `ProviderAuth` → `./auth`\n- `ProviderError` → `./error`\n- `ModelsDev` → `./models`\n- `ProviderTransform` → `./transform`\n\n---\n\n### 3. `packages/opencode/src/provider/provider.ts`（核心文件，~1000行）\n**核心功能**：Provider 系统的核心实现，负责管理所有 AI 模型提供方的注册、初始化、模型加载和语言模型实例化。\n\n**关键逻辑**：\n1. **BUNDLED_PROVIDERS**：内置了 20+ 个 AI SDK 提供方的动态导入映射（如 OpenAI、Anthropic、Google、Azure、Bedrock、DeepSeek 等），每个提供方通过 `createXxx()` 工厂函数创建 SDK 实例。\n2. **custom() 函数**：为每个提供方定义自定义行为，包括：\n   - **autoload**：是否自动加载\n   - **getModel**：自定义模型获取逻辑（如 GitHub Copilot 根据模型版本选择 Chat API 或 Responses API）\n   - **vars**：环境变量注入\n   - **options**：额外配置（如 API Key、Headers）\n   - **discoverModels**：动态发现模型（如 GitLab）\n3. **状态初始化（state）**：\n   - 从 `models.dev` 获取模型数据库\n   - 合并配置文件中的提供方配置\n   - 加载环境变量中的 API Key\n   - 加载已认证的 API Key\n   - 执行插件钩子\n   - 过滤已禁用/已弃用/Alpha 状态的模型\n4. **resolveSDK()**：解析并缓存 SDK 实例，处理：\n   - baseURL 模板变量替换（`${VAR}`）\n   - 自定义 fetch 实现（含 chunk 超时、信号合并）\n   - OpenAI itemId 剥离（模仿 Codex 行为）\n   - SSE 流超时包装\n5. **getLanguage()**：获取 `LanguageModelV3` 实例，优先使用自定义 modelLoader，否则调用 `sdk.languageModel()`\n6. **defaultModel()**：按优先级选择默认模型：配置文件 → 最近使用 → 排序第一个\n7. **getSmallModel()**：按优先级列表选择轻量模型（如 claude-haiku、gpt-5-nano）\n8. **sort()**：模型排序优先级：gpt-5 > claude-sonnet-4 > big-pickle > gemini-3-pro\n\n---\n\n### 4. `packages/opencode/src/provider/auth.ts`\n**核心功能**：提供方认证管理，支持 OAuth 和 API Key 两种认证方式。\n\n**关键逻辑**：\n1. **Method Schema**：定义认证方法类型（oauth/api），包含提示信息（文本输入/选择）\n2. **authorize()**：发起 OAuth 授权流程，支持带验证的提示输入\n3. **callback()**：处理 OAuth 回调，支持 code 和 auto 两种模式\n4. **状态管理**：维护待处理的 OAuth 请求映射\n5. **错误处理**：定义了 OauthMissing、OauthCodeMissing、OauthCallbackFailed、ValidationFailed 等错误类型\n\n---\n\n### 5. `packages/opencode/src/provider/error.ts`\n**核心功能**：API 调用错误的解析与分类。\n\n**关键逻辑**：\n1. **OVERFLOW_PATTERNS**：包含 20+ 个正则表达式，用于检测上下文溢出错误（覆盖 Anthropic、OpenAI、Google、xAI、Groq、DeepSeek 等主流提供方）\n2. **parseAPICallError()**：将 `APICallError` 解析为结构化错误：\n   - `context_overflow`：上下文溢出\n   - `api_error`：一般 API 错误（含可重试标记）\n3. **parseStreamError()**：解析流式响应中的错误，处理 `context_length_exceeded`、`insufficient_quota`、`usage_not_included`、`invalid_prompt` 等错误码\n4. **message()**：智能提取错误消息，处理 HTML 响应体（网关/代理错误页）\n\n---\n\n### 6. `packages/opencode/src/provider/models.ts`\n**核心功能**：从 `models.dev` 获取模型数据，支持缓存和定时刷新。\n\n**关键逻辑**：\n1. **数据源**：默认从 `https://models.dev/api.json` 获取，可通过 `OPENCODE_MODELS_URL` 环境变量覆盖\n2. **缓存策略**：本地缓存 5 分钟 TTL，使用文件锁防止并发写入\n3. **构建时快照**：支持通过 `models-snapshot.js` 嵌入构建时数据\n4. **定时刷新**：每小时自动刷新一次\n5. **Schema 定义**：定义了 `Model` 和 `Provider` 的 Zod Schema，包含模型 ID、名称、成本、限制、能力、模态等完整信息\n\n---\n\n### 7. `packages/opencode/src/provider/models-snapshot.d.ts`\n**核心功能**：构建时生成的模型快照的类型声明文件，声明 `snapshot: Record<string, unknown>`。\n\n---\n\n### 8. `packages/opencode/src/provider/schema.ts`\n**核心功能**：定义品牌类型 `ProviderID` 和 `ModelID`，提供 Zod Schema 和预定义的知名提供方常量。\n\n**关键逻辑**：\n- `ProviderID`：字符串品牌类型，预定义了 opencode、anthropic、openai、google、github-copilot、amazon-bedrock 等 12 个知名提供方\n- `ModelID`：字符串品牌类型\n\n---\n\n### 9. `packages/opencode/src/provider/transform.ts`（核心文件）\n**核心功能**：消息转换、推理配置、工具准备、缓存策略等预处理逻辑。\n\n**关键逻辑**：\n1. **normalizeMessages()**：消息规范化：\n   - Anthropic/Bedrock：过滤空内容消息\n   - Claude：清理 toolCallId 中的特殊字符\n   - Anthropic：重新排序 assistant 消息（tool_use 块后不能跟非 tool 内容）\n   - Mistral：清理 toolCallId，插入占位 assistant 消息修复消息序列\n   - 推理内容处理：将 reasoning 部分提取到 providerOptions 中\n2. **applyCaching()**：为 Anthropic/OpenRouter/Bedrock 等提供方添加缓存控制标记\n3. **unsupportedParts()**：检测并替换模型不支持的多模态输入（如图片、音频、视频、PDF）\n4. **variants()**：为推理模型生成推理努力度变体配置，覆盖 20+ 个 SDK 提供方：\n   - OpenAI：支持 none/minimal/low/medium/high/xhigh\n   - Anthropic：支持 adaptive thinking + budgetTokens\n   - Google：支持 thinkingConfig/thinkingLevel\n   - Bedrock：支持 reasoningConfig\n   - 等等\n5. **options()**：生成模型调用选项，包括 store、reasoningEffort、textVerbosity、thinking 等\n6. **smallOptions()**：为轻量模型生成简化选项\n7. **providerOptions()**：将选项路由到正确的 providerOptions 命名空间\n8. **schema()**：为 Google/Gemini 模型清理 JSON Schema（整数枚举转字符串、移除不支持的属性）\n\n---\n\n### 10. `packages/opencode/src/provider/sdk/copilot/`（SDK 层）\n\n#### 10.1 `copilot-provider.ts`\n**核心功能**：创建 OpenAI 兼容的 Provider 实例工厂。\n\n**关键逻辑**：\n- `createOpenaiCompatible()`：创建 Provider 实例，支持 Chat 和 Responses 两种 API\n- 自动添加 `Authorization: Bearer` 头\n- 支持自定义 baseURL、headers、fetch 实现\n- 提供 `chat()`、`responses()`、`languageModel()` 三种模型创建方法\n\n#### 10.2 `chat/openai-compatible-chat-language-model.ts`\n**核心功能**：Chat Completions API 的 LanguageModelV3 实现。\n\n**关键逻辑**：\n- **doGenerate()**：非流式生成，解析响应中的 text、reasoning_text、tool_calls\n- **doStream()**：流式生成，处理 SSE 事件流\n- 支持 Copilot 特有的 `reasoning_text` 和 `reasoning_opaque` 字段\n- 处理 tool_calls 的增量构建（支持分块传输）\n- 管理 reasoning 和 text 的交替输出\n\n#### 10.3 `responses/openai-responses-language-model.ts`\n**核心功能**：OpenAI Responses API 的 LanguageModelV3 实现（~600行）。\n\n**关键逻辑**：\n- **doGenerate()**：处理完整的 Responses API 响应，支持：\n  - 消息输出（含 URL 引用、文件引用）\n  - 推理内容（含加密内容和摘要）\n  - 函数调用\n  - 内置工具：web_search、file_search、code_interpreter、image_generation、local_shell、computer_use\n- **doStream()**：处理 20+ 种 SSE 事件类型：\n  - `response.created`、`response.completed`、`response.incomplete`\n  - `response.output_item.added`、`response.output_item.done`\n  - `response.output_text.delta`\n  - `response.function_call_arguments.delta`\n  - `response.reasoning_summary_part.added`、`response.reasoning_summary_text.delta`\n  - `response.code_interpreter_call_code.delta/done`\n  - `response.image_generation_call.partial_image`\n  - `response.output_text.annotation.added`\n  - `error`\n- **getResponsesModelConfig()**：根据模型 ID 判断是否为推理模型、系统消息模式、是否支持 flex/priority 处理\n\n#### 10.4 `responses/convert-to-openai-responses-input.ts`\n**核心功能**：将通用 Prompt 转换为 Responses API 输入格式。\n\n**关键逻辑**：\n- 处理 system/developer/user/assistant/tool 角色\n- 文件上传：支持 URL、base64、file_id 三种方式\n- 推理内容：使用 item_reference 或完整推理对象\n- 工具调用：支持 function_call、local_shell_call、mcp_approval_response\n- 处理 provider-executed 工具的结果引用\n\n#### 10.5 `responses/openai-responses-prepare-tools.ts`\n**核心功能**：将通用工具定义转换为 Responses API 工具格式。\n\n**关键逻辑**：\n- 支持 function、file_search、web_search、web_search_preview、code_interpreter、image_generation、local_shell 七种工具类型\n- 解析各工具的特定参数 Schema\n- 处理 toolChoice 映射\n\n#### 10.6 `responses/tool/` 目录\n**核心功能**：定义各内置工具的输入/输出 Schema 和工厂函数。\n\n| 文件 | 工具 | 关键参数 |\n|------|------|---------|\n| `code-interpreter.ts` | 代码解释器 | code, containerId, outputs(logs/image) |\n| `file-search.ts` | 文件搜索 | vectorStoreIds, maxNumResults, ranking, filters |\n| `image-generation.ts` | 图像生成 | background, inputFidelity, model, quality, size, outputFormat |\n| `local-shell.ts` | 本地 Shell | command, timeoutMs, user, workingDirectory, env |\n| `web-search-preview.ts` | 网页搜索预览 | searchContextSize, userLocation |\n| `web-search.ts` | 网页搜索 | filters(allowedDomains), searchContextSize, userLocation |\n\n---\n\n## 三、整体架构总结\n\n这是一个 **AI 模型提供方（Provider）抽象层**，设计用于 opencode 编辑器（类似 GitHub Copilot/Codex）的底层 AI 调用基础设施：\n\n1. **分层架构**：\n   - **Provider 层**（`provider.ts`）：管理所有 AI 提供方的注册、初始化、模型发现\n   - **认证层**（`auth.ts`）：处理 OAuth 和 API Key 认证\n   - **模型数据层**（`models.ts`）：从远程获取模型元数据\n   - **转换层**（`transform.ts`）：消息预处理、推理配置、Schema 适配\n   - **SDK 层**（`sdk/copilot/`）：实现 OpenAI Chat Completions 和 Responses API 的兼容适配\n\n2. **支持 20+ 个 AI 提供方**：OpenAI、Anthropic、Google、Azure、AWS Bedrock、DeepSeek、Mistral、Groq、xAI、Cohere、Perplexity、GitHub Copilot、GitLab、Cloudflare、OpenRouter 等\n\n3. **核心能力**：\n   - 多模态输入（文本、图像、音频、视频、PDF）\n   - 推理/思考链支持（多种推理努力度配置）\n   - 工具调用（函数调用 + 内置工具）\n   - 流式和非流式生成\n   - 缓存控制\n   - 错误分类与重试策略\n\n\n--- 关键代码片段 1 ---\n{\n  \"name\": \"opencode-provider\",\n  \"private\": true,\n  \"description\": \"Minimal opencode Provider source for experiment reproduction\"\n}\n\n\n--- 关键代码片段 2 ---\n{\n  \"compilerOptions\": {\n    \"target\": \"ESNext\",\n    \"module\": \"ESNext\",\n    \"strict\": true\n  }\n}\n\n\n--- 关键代码片段 3 ---\n# opencode Provider\n\nMinimal source files from opencode's Provider system, used for tool calling reasoning language drift experiment reproduction.\n\n\n\n原始任务：请分析 opencode 项目的 Provider 系统，了解它是怎么加载和管理 AI Provider 的。",
		"role": "user"

	{
		"carry_reasoning": true,
		"content": "# opencode Provider 系统分析报告\n\n## 一、整体架构概览\n\nopencode 的 Provider 系统是一个**通用 AI 模型提供方抽象层**，设计用于统一管理多个 AI 服务商的模型接入。它的核心职责是：\n\n1. **注册与管理** 20+ 个 AI 提供方（OpenAI、Anthropic、Google、Bedrock、GitHub Copilot 等）\n2. **动态加载** SDK 包，按需实例化 Language Model\n3. **模型发现** 与 **元数据管理**（能力、定价、限速、变体）\n4. **认证管理**（OAuth / API Key）\n5. **消息预处理** 与 **SDK 差异适配**\n\n架构分为四层：\n\n```\n┌─────────────────────────────────────────────┐\n│                Provider 层                   │\n│        (provider.ts - 核心编排器)             │\n├─────────────────────────────────────────────┤\n│              认证层 & 模型数据层               │\n│        (auth.ts, models.ts)                  │\n├─────────────────────────────────────────────┤\n│              转换/适配层                      │\n│        (transform.ts, error.ts)             │\n├─────────────────────────────────────────────┤\n│               SDK 实现层                      │\n│   (sdk/copilot/ - Chat + Responses API)      │\n└─────────────────────────────────────────────┘\n```\n\n---\n\n## 二、核心文件逐层分析\n\n### 1. Provider 层（`provider.ts`）- 大脑\n\n这是整个系统最核心的文件（~1000 行），实现了以下关键机制：\n\n#### a) 内置提供方注册表 `BUNDLED_PROVIDERS`\n\n```typescript\nconst BUNDLED_PROVIDERS: Record<string, () => Promise<(opts: any) => BundledSDK>> = {\n  \"@ai-sdk/openai\": () => import(\"@ai-sdk/openai\").then(m => m.createOpenAI),\n  \"@ai-sdk/anthropic\": () => import(\"@ai-sdk/anthropic\").then(m => m.createAnthropic),\n  \"@ai-sdk/google\": () => import(\"@ai-sdk/google\").then(m => m.createGoogleGenerativeAI),\n  // ... 共 20+ 个提供方\n  \"@ai-sdk/github-copilot\": () => import(\"./sdk/copilot\").then(m => m.createOpenaiCompatible),\n}\n```\n\n每个提供方通过 **动态 `import()`** 懒加载，SDK 工厂函数接收 `${ providerID, apiKey, baseURL, ...options }` 参数，返回 `BundledSDK`（包含 `languageModel()` 方法）。\n\n#### b) 自定义行为注入 `custom()`\n\n为每个提供方定义专有的加载行为，示例如下：\n\n| 提供方 | 自定义行为 |\n|--------|-----------|\n| **GitHub Copilot** | 根据模型版本选择 Chat API (`gpt-4` 等) 或 Responses API (`gpt-5+`)，通过 `shouldUseCopilotResponsesApi()` 判断 |\n| **Azure** | 从环境变量或配置中读取 `AZURE_RESOURCE_NAME`，注入到 baseURL 模板 `\\${AZURE_RESOURCE_NAME}` |\n| **Amazon Bedrock** | 复杂的地域前缀逻辑（`us.`、`eu.`、`apac.`、`au.`、`jp.`），按模型家族和区域自动添加前缀 |\n| **Google Vertex** | 自动获取 GCP 凭据（`google-auth-library`），注入 `project`、`location` 和自定义 `fetch` |\n| **Cloudflare AI Gateway** | 使用 `ai-gateway-provider` 包创建统一网关，通过 `createUnified()` 实现多模型路由 |\n| **GitLab** | 支持动态模型发现（`discoverModels()`），从 Duo Agent Platform API 获取工作流模型 |\n| **opencode** | 默认开放模型（`apiKey: \"public\"`），无 API Key 时只保留免费模型 |\n\n#### c) Provider 状态初始化流程（`layer` 函数）\n\n完整的初始化序列：\n\n```\n1. 加载插件 (plugin.list())\n2. 读取配置文件 cfg.provider (opencode.json)\n3. 从 models.dev 获取模型数据库 (ModelsDev.get())\n4. 合并配置中定义的模型覆盖\n5. 从环境变量中发现已配置的 Provider\n6. 从已认证的 API Keys 中发现 Provider\n7. 执行插件 auth hook\n8. 执行 custom() 自定义加载逻辑\n9. 重应用配置文件覆盖\n10. 执行 GitLab 动态模型发现\n11. 执行插件 provider hook (替换/补充模型列表)\n12. 过滤：disabled provider / alpha 模型 / deprecated 模型 / blacklist/whitelist\n13. 生成模型变体配置 (variants)\n```\n\n#### d) SDK 解析与缓存 `resolveSDK()`\n\n```\nresolveSDK(model, state, envs)\n  ├── 合并 provider.options + model.headers\n  ├── 替换 baseURL 中的模板变量 (${ENV_VAR})\n  ├── 设置 apiKey（来自 provider.key 或 options）\n  ├── 计算缓存 key = Hash.fast(JSON.stringify({ providerID, npm, options }))\n  ├── 检查缓存 → 直接返回\n  ├── 构建自定义 fetch（支持 chunkTimeout、AbortSignal.any 合并）\n  ├── 尝试 BUNDLED_PROVIDERS → 动态 import 工厂\n  └── 否则 → Npm.add() 安装 → 动态 import → 调用 createXxx() 工厂\n```\n\n关键优化：**SDK 实例缓存**，以 `(providerID, npm包名, options)` 三元组作为 key，避免重复创建。\n\n#### e) Language Model 获取 `getLanguage()`\n\n```typescript\nconst language = s.modelLoaders[model.providerID]\n  ? await s.modelLoaders[model.providerID](sdk, model.api.id, { ...provider.options, ...model.options })\n  : sdk.languageModel(model.api.id)\n```\n\n优先使用自定义的 `modelLoader`（如 Bedrock 的地域前缀逻辑），否则调用标准 `sdk.languageModel()`。\n\n---\n\n### 2. 认证层（`auth.ts`）\n\n支持两种认证模式：\n\n| 模式 | 流程 |\n|------|------|\n| **OAuth** | 1. `methods()` 获取认证方法列表 → 2. `authorize()` 发起 OAuth → 3. `callback()` 处理回调，保存 access/refresh token |\n| **API Key** | 直接通过 `auth.set()` 存储 key |\n\n认证信息通过 **插件系统** 注入，插件声明 `auth.provider` 和对应的 loader 函数。\n\n---\n\n### 3. 模型数据层（`models.ts`）\n\n数据流：\n\n```\nmodels.dev (远程 /api.json)\n    ↓ 定时刷新 (5min TTL)\n本地缓存 (models.json)\n    ↓ 构建时\nmodels-snapshot.js (内嵌快照)\n    ↓\nModelsDev.get() → Record<string, Provider>\n```\n\n每个 Provider 包含其下所有模型的完整元数据：ID、名称、家族、成本（input/output/cache）、限制（context/output）、能力（temperature/reasoning/toolcall）、模态（text/image/audio/video/pdf）、状态（alpha/beta/deprecated/active）等。\n\n---\n\n### 4. 转换适配层（`transform.ts`）\n\n核心预处理管道，按以下顺序执行：\n\n```\nmessage(msgs, model, options)\n  ├── 1. unsupportedParts() - 检测并替换不支持的模态输入\n  ├── 2. normalizeMessages() - 各 SDK 的特殊消息处理\n  │   ├── Anthropic: 过滤空内容，重排 assistant 消息顺序\n  │   ├── Mistral: 清理 toolCallId (9字符字母数字)，插入占位 assistant\n  │   ├── DeepSeek: 保留 reasoning part，注入 providerOptions\n  │   └── 通用: 将 reasoning 提取到 providerOptions.reasoning_content\n  └── 3. applyCaching() - 为 Anthropic/OpenRouter/Bedrock 注入缓存标记\n```\n\n此外还负责：\n- **variants()**: 为每个推理模型生成不同推理努力度的变体配置（覆盖 20+ SDK）\n- **options()**: 生成模型调用选项（store、reasoningEffort、textVerbosity、thinking 等）\n- **schema()**: 为 Google/Gemini 清理 JSON Schema（整数枚举转字符串）\n\n---\n\n### 5. SDK 实现层（`sdk/copilot/`）\n\n#### 两套 API 实现\n\n**Chat Completions API**（传统实现）：\n- `openai-compatible-chat-language-model.ts`\n- 支持 `reasoning_text`、`reasoning_opaque`（Copilot 特有）\n- Tool calls 增量构建\n- Reasoning ↔ Text 交替输出管理\n\n**Responses API**（新版，`gpt-5+`）：\n- `openai-responses-language-model.ts` (~600行)\n- 处理 20+ 种 SSE 事件类型\n- 内置工具：web_search、file_search、code_interpreter、image_generation、local_shell、computer_use\n- 推理内容加密支持（`encrypted_content`）\n- 自动多摘要片段管理\n\n#### 工具定义（`responses/tool/`）\n\n| 工具 | 输入 Schema | 输出 Schema |\n|------|-------------|-------------|\n| code-interpreter | code, containerId | logs[] + image[] |\n| file-search | vectorStoreIds, maxNumResults, ranking, filters | queries[] + results[] |\n| image-generation | background, model, quality, size, outputFormat | result (base64) |\n| local-shell | command, timeoutMs, user, workingDirectory, env | output |\n| web-search-preview | searchContextSize, userLocation | (无结构化输出) |\n| web-search | filters, searchContextSize, userLocation | (无结构化输出) |\n\n---\n\n### 6. 错误处理层（`error.ts`）\n\n智能解析 API 错误，分类为两种：\n\n```typescript\ntype ParsedAPICallError =\n  | { type: \"context_overflow\"; message: string }\n  | { type: \"api_error\"; message: string; statusCode: number; isRetryable: boolean }\n```\n\n- 20+ 个正则表达式检测上下文溢出（覆盖所有主流提供方）\n- 智能提取错误消息（处理 HTML 响应体 / 空消息 / JSON body）\n- 流式错误解析（`context_length_exceeded`、`insufficient_quota` 等）\n\n---\n\n## 三、整体数据流（用户请求举例）\n\n用户发送一条带图片的消息给 `gpt-5` 模型：\n\n```\n1. 解析模型ID \"openai/gpt-5\" → providerID=\"openai\", modelID=\"gpt-5\"\n2. getModel(\"openai\", \"gpt-5\") → 从 provider 状态中查找模型元数据\n3. getLanguage(model) → resolveSDK() 创建/获取缓存的 OpenAI SDK\n4. transform.message() 预处理：\n   - 检查模型是否支持图片输入 ✓\n   - 将 reasoning 部分提取到 providerOptions\n   - 设置 store=false, reasoningEffort=\"medium\", textVerbosity=\"low\"\n5. sdk.responses(modelID).doStream(options)\n   - 将 Prompt 转换为 Responses API 输入格式\n   - 发送 POST /responses + stream:true\n   - 处理 SSE 事件流：推理摘要 → 文本增量 → 工具调用\n6. 错误发生时 parseAPICallError() 分类并决定是否重试\n```\n\n---\n\n## 四、设计亮点\n\n1. **分层解耦**：认证、模型数据、SDK 实现、业务逻辑完全分离\n2. **动态加载**：SDK 包按需 `import()`，不增加启动体积\n3. **实例缓存**：SDK 实例以 `(providerID, npm, options)` 三元组缓存，避免重复创建\n4. **模板变量**：baseURL 支持 `${ENV_VAR}` 和 `${PROVIDER_VAR}` 动态替换\n5. **自定义 fetch**：支持 chunk 超时、信号合并、OpenAI itemId 剥离\n6. **推理变体**：为每个推理模型自动生成多种推理努力度配置\n7. **SSE 超时**：`wrapSSE()` 确保流式读取不会永久挂起",
		"reasoning": "The user wants me to analyze the opencode project's Provider system and understand how it loads and manages AI Providers. I've already explored the entire codebase thoroughly. Let me synthesize a comprehensive analysis.",
		"role": "assistant",
		"tool_calls": []
	}
]

\"number\" || ms <= 0) return res\n  if (!res.body) return res\n  if (!res.headers.get(\"content-type\")?.includes(\"text/event-stream\")) return res\n\n  const reader = res.body.getReader()\n  const body = new ReadableStream<Uint8Array>({\n    async pull(ctrl) {\n      const part = await new Promise<Awaited<ReturnType<typeof reader.read>>>((resolve, reject) => {\n        const id = setTimeout(() => {\n          const err = new Error(\"SSE read timed out\")\n          ctl.abort(err)\n          void reader.cancel(err)\n          reject(err)\n        }, ms)\n\n        reader.read().then(\n          (part) => {\n            clearTimeout(id)\n            resolve(part)\n          },\n          (err) => {\n            clearTimeout(id)\n            reject(err)\n          },\n        )\n      })\n\n      if (part.done) {\n        ctrl.close()\n        return\n      }\n\n      ctrl.enqueue(part.value)\n    },\n    async cancel(reason) {\n      ctl.abort(reason)\n      await reader.cancel(reason)\n    },\n  })\n\n  return new Response(body, {\n    headers: new Headers(res.headers),\n    status: res.status,\n    statusText: res.statusText,\n  })\n}\n\ntype BundledSDK = {\n },\n  }\n  if (c?.context_over_200k) {\n    result.experimentalOver200K = {\n      cache: {\n        read: c.context_over_200k.cache_read ?? 0,\n        write: c.context_over_200k.cache_write ?? 0,\n      },\n      input: c.context_over_200k.input,\n      output: c.context_over_200k.output,\n    }\n  }\n  return result\n}\n\nfunction fromModelsDevModel(provider: ModelsDev.Provider, model:   },\n      interleaved: model.interleaved ?? false,\n    },\n    release_date: model.release_date ?? \"\",\n    variants: {},\n  }\n\n  return {\n    ...base,\n    variants:    function mergeProvider(providerID: ProviderID, provider: Partial<Info>) {\n          const existing = providers[providerID]\n          if (existing) {\n            // @ts-expect-error\n            providers[providerID] = mergeDeep(existing, provider)\n            return\n          }\n          const match = database[providerID]\n          if (!match) return\n          // @ts-expect-error\n          providers[providerID] = mergeDeep(match, provider)\n        }\n\n        // load plugins first so config() hook runs before reading cfg.provider\n        const plugins = yield* plugin.list()\n\n        // now read config providers - includes any modifications from plugin config() hook\n        const configProviders = Object.entries(cfg.provider ?? {})\n        const disabled = new            id: ModelID.make(modelID),\n              api: {\n                id: model.id ?? existingModel?.api.id ?? modelID,\n                npm:\n                  model.provider?.npm ??\n                  provider.npm ??\n                  existingModel?.api.npm ??\n                  modelsDev[providerID]?.npm ??\n                  \"@ai-sdk/openai-compatible\",\n                url: model.provider?.api ?? provider?.api ?? existingModel?.api.url ?? modelsDev[providerID]?.api ?? \"\",\n              },\n              status: model.status ?? existingModel?.status ?? \"active\",\n              name,\n              providerID: ProviderID.make(providerID),\n              capabilities: {\n                temperature: model.temperature ?? existingModel?.capabilities.temperature ?? 		"content": "import { APICallError } from \"ai\"\nimport { STATUS_CODES } from \"http\"\nimport { iife } from \"@/util/iife\"\nimport type { ProviderID } from \"./schema\"\n\n// Adapted from overflow detection patterns in:\n// https://github.com/badlogic/pi-mono/blob/main/packages/ai/src/utils/overflow.ts\nconst OVERFLOW_PATTERNS = [\n  /prompt is too long/i, // Anthropic\n  /input is too long for requested model/i, // Amazon Bedrock\n  /exceeds the context window/i, // OpenAI (Completions + Responses API message text)\n  /input token count.*exceeds the maximum/i, // Google (Gemini)\n  /maximum prompt length is \\d+/i, // xAI (Grok)\n  /reduce the length of the messages/i, // Groq\n  /maximum context length is \\d+ tokens/i, // OpenRouter, DeepSeek, vLLM\n  /exceeds the limit of \\d+/i, // GitHub Copilot\n  /exceeds the available context size/i, // llama.cpp server\n  /greater than the context length/i, // LM Studio\n  /context window exceeds limit/i, // MiniMax\n  /exceeded model token limit/i, // Kimi For Coding, Moonshot\n  /context[_ ]length[_ ]exceeded/i, // Generic fallback\n  /request entity too large/i, // HTTP 413\n  /context length is only \\d+ tokens/i, // vLLM\n  /input length.*exceeds.*context length/i, // vLLM\n  /prompt too long; exceeded (?:max )?context length/i, // Ollama explicit overflow error\n  /too large for model with \\d+ maximum context length/i, // Mistral\n  /model_context_window_exceeded/i, // z.ai non-standard finish_reason surfaced as error text\n]\n\nfunction isOpenAiErrorRetryable(e: APICallError) {\n  const status = e.statusCode\n  if (!status) return e.isRetryable\n  // openai sometimes returns 404 for models that are actually available\n  return status === 404 || e.isRetryable\n}\n\n// Providers not reliably handled in this function:\n// - z.ai: can accept overflow silently (needs token-count/context-window checks)\nfunction isOverflow(message: string) {\n  if (OVERFLOW_PATTERNS.some((p) => p.test(message))) return true\n\n  // Providers/status patterns handled outside of regex list:\n  // - Cerebras: often returns \"400 (no body)\" / \"413 (no body)\"\n  // - Mistral: often returns \"400 (no body)\" / \"413 (no body)\"\n  return /^4(00|13)\\s*(status code)?\\s*\\(no body\\)/i.test(message)\n}\n\nfunction message(providerID: ProviderID, e: APICallError) {\n  return iife(() => {\n    const msg = e.message\n    if (msg === \"\") {\n      if (e.responseBody) return e.responseBody\n      if (e.statusCode) {\n        const err = STATUS_CODES[e.statusCode]\n        if (err) return err\n      }\n      return \"Unknown error\"\n    }\n\n    if (!e.responseBody || (e.statusCode && msg !== STATUS_CODES[e.statusCode])) {\n      return msg\n    }\n\n    try {\n      const body = JSON.parse(e.responseBody)\n      // try to extract common error message fields\n      const errMsg = body.message || body.error || body.error?.message\n      if (errMsg && typeof errMsg === \"string\") {\n        return `${msg}: ${errMsg}`\n      }\n    } catch {}\n\n    // If responseBody is HTML (e.g. from a gateway or proxy error page),\n    // provide a human-readable message instead of dumping raw markup\n    if (/^\\s*<!doctype|^\\s*<html/i.test(e.responseBody)) {\n      if (e.statusCode === 401) {\n        return \"Unauthorized: request was blocked by a gateway or proxy. Your authentication token may be missing or expired — try running `opencode auth login <your provider URL>` to re-authenticate.\"\n      }\n      if (e.statusCode === 403) {\n        return \"Forbidden: request was blocked by a gateway or proxy. You may not have permission to access this resource — check your account and provider settings.\"\n      }\n      return msg\n    }\n\n    return `${msg}: ${e.responseBody}`\n  }).trim()\n}\n\nfunction json(input: unknown) {\n  if (typeof input === \"string\") {\n    try {\n      const result = JSON.parse(input)\n      if (result && typeof result === \"object\") return result\n      return undefined\n    } catch {\n      return undefined\n    }\n  }\n  if (typeof input === \"object\" && input !== null) {\n    return input\n  }\n  return undefined\n}\n\nexport type ParsedStreamError =\n  | {\n      type: \"context_overflow\"\n      message: string\n      responseBody: string\n    }\n  | {\n      type: \"api_error\"\n      message: string\n      isRetryable: false\n      responseBody: string\n    }\n\nexport function parseStreamError(input: unknown): ParsedStreamError | undefined {\n  const body = json(input)\n  if (!body) return\n\n  const responseBody = JSON.stringify(body)\n  if (body.type !== \"error\") return\n\n  switch (body?.error?.code) {\n    case \"context_length_exceeded\":\n      return {\n        type: \"context_overflow\",\n        message: \"Input exceeds context window of this model\",\n        responseBody,\n      }\n    case \"insufficient_quota\":\n      return {\n        type: \"api_error\",\n        message: \"Quota exceeded. Check your plan and billing details.\",\n        isRetryable: false,\n        responseBody,\n      }\n    case \"usage_not_included\":\n      return {\n        type: \"api_error\",\n        message: \"To use Codex with your ChatGPT plan, upgrade to Plus: https://chatgpt.com/explore/plus.\",\n        isRetryable: false,\n        responseBody,\n      }\n    case \"invalid_prompt\":\n      return {\n        type: \"api_error\",\n        message: typeof body?.error?.message === \"string\" ? body?.error?.message : \"Invalid prompt.\",\n        isRetryable: false,\n        responseBody,\n      }\n  }\n}\n\nexport type ParsedAPICallError =\n  | {\n      type: \"context_overflow\"\n      message: string\n      responseBody?: string\n    }\n  | {\n      type: \"api_error\"\n      message: string\n      statusCode?: number\n      isRetryable: boolean\n      responseHeaders?: Record<string, string>\n      responseBody?: string\n      metadata?: Record<string, string>\n    }\n\nexport function parseAPICallError(input: { providerID: ProviderID; error: APICallError }): ParsedAPICallError {\n  const m = message(input.providerID, input.error)\n  const body = json(input.error.responseBody)\n  if (isOverflow(m) || input.error.statusCode === 413 || body?.error?.code === \"context_length_exceeded\") {\n    return {\n      type: \"context_overflow\",\n      message: m,\n      responseBody: input.error.responseBody,\n    }\n  }\n\n  const metadata = input.error.url ? { url: input.error.url } : undefined\n  return {\n    type: \"api_error\",\n    message: m,\n    statusCode: input.error.statusCode,\n    isRetryable: input.providerID.startsWith(\"openai\") ? isOpenAiErrorRetryable(input.error) : input.error.isRetryable,\n    responseHeaders: input.error.responseHeaders,\n    responseBody: input.error.responseBody,\n    metadata,\n  }\n}\n",

switch (npm) {\n    case \"@ai-sdk/github-copilot\":\n      return \"copilot\"\n    case \"@ai-sdk/azure\":\n      return \"azure\"\n    case \"@ai-sdk/openai\":\n      return \"openai\"\n    case case \"@openrouter/ai-sdk-provider\":\n      return \"openrouter\"\n  }\n  return undefined\n}\n\n// Returns the providerOptions key that the AI SDK expects for the given model.\n// Note: regardless of the provider's instantiated name.\nfunction providerOptionsKey(model: Provider.Model): string {\n  // @ai-sdk/openai-compatible's getOpenAIMetadata() hardcodes \"openaiCompatible\"\n  // Any provider wrapping\n  // openai-compatible (e.g., @openrouter/ai-sdk-provider) inherits this behavior.\n  const npm = model.api.npm\n  if (npm === \"@ai-sdk/openai-compatible\" || npm ===
