     return \"vertex\"\n    case \"@ai-sdk/google\":\n      return \"google\"\n    case \"@ai-sdk/deepseek\":\n      return \"deepseek\"\n    case \"@ai-sdk/gateway\":\n      return \"gateway\"\n    case \"@openrouter/ai-sdk-provider\":\n      return \"openrouter\"\n  }\n  return undefined\n}\n\n// Returns the providerOptions key that the AI SDK expects for the given model.\n// Note: @ai-sdk/openai-compatible's getOpenAIMetadata() hardcodes \"openaiCompatible\"\n// as the providerOptions key (see node_modules/@ai-sdk/openai-compatible/dist/index.mjs),\n// so we must use that key regardless of the provider's instantiated name.\nfunction providerOptionsKey(model: Provider.Model): string {\n  // @ai-sdk/openai-compatible's getOpenAIMetadata() hardcodes \"openaiCompatible\"\n  // as the providerOptions key for reasoning content. Any provider wrapping\n  // openai-compatible (e.g., @openrouter/ai-sdk-provider) inherits this behavior.\n  const npm = model.api.npm\n  if (npm === \"@ai-sdk/openai-compatible\" || npm === \"@openrouter/ai-sdk-provider\") {\n    return \"openaiCompatible\"\n  }\n  return sdkKey(npm) ?? \"openaiCompatible\"\n}\n\nfunction normalizeMessages(\n  msgs: ModelMessage[],\n  model: Provider.Model,\n  _options: Record<string, unknown>,\n): ModelMessage[] {\n  // Anthropic rejects messages with empty content - filter out empty string messages\n  // and remove empty text/reasoning parts from array content\n  if (model.api.npm === \"@ai-sdk/anthropic\" || model.api.npm === \"@ai-sdk/amazon-bedrock\") {\n    msgs = msgs\n      .map((msg) => {\n        if (typeof msg.content === \"string\") {\n          if (msg.content === \"\") return undefined\n          return msg\n        }\n        if (!Array.isArray(msg.content)) return msg\n        const filtered = msg.content.filter((part) => {\n          if (part.type === \"text\" || part.type === \"reasoning\") {\n            return part.text !== \"\"\n          }\n          return true\n        })\n        if (filtered.length === 0) return undefined\n        return { ...msg, content: filtered }\n      })\n      .filter((msg): msg is ModelMessage => msg !== undefined && msg.content !== \"\")\n  }\n\n  if (model.api.id.includes(\"claude\")) {\n    const scrub = (id: string) => id.replace(/[^a-zA-Z0-9_-]/g, \"_\")\n    msgs = msgs.map((msg) => {\n      if (msg.role === \"assistant\" && Array.isArray(msg.content)) {\n        return {\n          ...msg,\n          content: msg.content.map((part) => {\n            if (part.type === \"tool-call\" || part.type === \"tool-result\") {\n              return { ...part, toolCallId: scrub(part.toolCallId) }\n            }\n            return part\n          }),\n        }\n      }\n      if (msg.role === \"tool\" && Array.isArray(msg.content)) {\n        return {\n          ...msg,\n          content: msg.content.map((part) => {\n            if (part.type === \"tool-result\") {\n              return { ...part, toolCallId: scrub(part.toolCallId) }\n            }\n            return part\n          }),\n        }\n      }\n      return msg\n    })\n  }\n  if ([\"@ai-sdk/anthropic\", \"@ai-sdk/google-vertex/anthropic\"].includes(model.api.npm)) {\n    // Anthropic rejects assistant turns where tool_use blocks are followed by non-tool\n    // content, e.g. [tool_use, tool_use, text], with:\n    // `tool_use` ids were found without `tool_result` blocks immediately after...\n    //\n    // Reorder that invalid shape into [text] + [tool_use, tool_use]. Consecutive\n    // assistant messages are later merged by the provider/SDK, so preserving the\n    // original [tool_use...] then [text] order still produces the invalid payload.\n    //\n    // The root cause appears to be somewhere upstream where the stream is originally\n    // processed. We were unable to locate an exact narrower reproduction elsewhere,\n    // so we keep this transform in place for the time being.\n    msgs = msgs.flatMap((msg) => {\n      if (msg.role !== \"assistant\" || !Array.isArray(msg.content)) return [msg]\n\n      const parts = msg.content\n      const first = parts.findIndex((part) => part.type === \"tool-call\")\n      if (first === -1) return [msg]\n      if (!parts.slice(first).some((part) => part.type !== \"tool-call\")) return [msg]\n      return [\n        { ...msg, content: parts.filter((part) => part.type !== \"tool-call\") },\n        { ...msg, content: parts.filter((part) => part.type === \"tool-call\") },\n      ]\n    })\n  }\n  if (\n    model.providerID === \"mistral\" ||\n    model.api.id.toLowerCase().includes(\"mistral\") ||\n    model.api.id.toLocaleLowerCase().includes(\"devstral\")\n  ) {\n    const scrub = (id: string) => {\n      return id\n        .replace(/[^a-zA-Z0-9]/g, \"\") // Remove non-alphanumeric characters\n        .substring(0, 9) // Take first 9 characters\n        .padEnd(9, \"0\") // Pad with zeros if less than 9 characters\n    }\n    const result: ModelMessage[] = []\n    for (let i = 0; i < msgs.length; i++) {\n      const msg = msgs[i]\n      const nextMsg = msgs[i + 1]\n\n      if (msg.role === \"assistant\" && Array.isArray(msg.content)) {\n        msg.content = msg.content.map((part) => {\n          if (part.type === \"tool-call\" || part.type === \"tool-result\") {\n            return { ...part, toolCallId: scrub(part.toolCallId) }\n          }\n          return part\n        })\n      }\n      if (msg.role === \"tool\" && Array.isArray(msg.content)) {\n        msg.content = msg.content.map((part) => {\n          if (part.type === \"tool-result\") {\n            return { ...part, toolCallId: scrub(part.toolCallId) }\n          }\n          return part\n        })\n      }\n      result.push(msg)\n\n      // Fix message sequence: tool messages cannot be followed by user messages\n      if (msg.role === \"tool\" && nextMsg?.role === \"user\") {\n        result.push({\n          role: \"assistant\",\n          content: [\n            {\n              type: \"text\",\n              text: \"Done.\",\n            },\n          ],\n        })\n      }\n    }\n    return result\n  }\n\n  // Detect whether the model uses reasoning/thinking and determine the\n  // providerOptions key/field for reasoning_content. For models without\n  // interleaved configured (e.g., DeepSeek via @ai-sdk/openai-compatible),\n  // default to the OpenAI-compatible reasoning_content field.\n  const interleaved = model.capabilities.interleaved\n  const isInterleaved = typeof interleaved === \"object\" && interleaved.field\n  const field = isInterleaved ? interleaved.field : \"reasoning_content\"\n  const key = providerOptionsKey(model)\n\n  // Check if we need to handle reasoning parts:\n  // - interleaved explicitly configured, OR\n  // - model has reasoning capability, OR\n  // - messages already contain reasoning parts (from DB replay)\n  const hasReasoningContent =\n    isInterleaved ||\n    model.capabilities.reasoning ||\n    msgs.some((msg) =>\n      msg.role === \"assistant\" &&\n      Array.isArray(msg.content) &&\n      msg.content.some((part: any) => part.type === \"reasoning\"),\n    )\n\n  if (hasReasoningContent) {\n    // @ai-sdk/deepseek 原生处理 reasoning，不走 providerOptions 注入。\n    // convertToDeepSeekChatMessages() 直接从 content 中读取 reasoning part，\n    // 不要剥离，保留在 content 数组里。\n    if (model.api.npm === \"@ai-sdk/deepseek\") {\n      return msgs.map((msg) => ({\n        ...msg,\n        providerOptions: {\n          ...msg.providerOptions,\n          [key]: {\n            ...msg.providerOptions?.[key],\n            thinking: { type: \"enabled\" },\n          },\n        },\n      }))\n    }\n\n    return msgs.map((msg) => {\n      if (msg.role === \"assistant\" && Array.isArray(msg.content)) {\n        const reasoningParts = msg.content.filter((part: any) => part.type === \"reasoning\")\n        const reasoningText = reasoningParts.map((part: any) => part.text).join(\"\")\n\n        // Filter out reasoning parts from content\n        const filteredContent = msg.content.filter((part: any) => part.type !== \"reasoning\")\n\n        // DeepSeek reasoning API requires ALL assistant messages in the conversation\n        // history to carry reasoning_content (even empty string). Old DB-replayed\n        // messages may have no reasoning parts at all — inject empty string for those.\n        return {\n          ...msg,\n          content: filteredContent,\n          providerOptions: {\n            ...msg.providerOptions,\n            [key]: {\n              ...msg.providerOptions?.[key],\n              [field]: reasoningText || \"\",\n            },\n          },\n        }\n      }\n\n      // Also handle string-content assistant messages (old DB format).\n      // Inject empty reasoning_content to satisfy DeepSeek API requirement.\n      if (msg.role === \"assistant\" && typeof msg.content === \"string\") {\n        return {\n          ...msg,\n          providerOptions: {\n            ...msg.providerOptions,\n            [key]: {\n              ...msg.providerOptions?.[key],\n              [field]: \"\",\n            },\n          },\n        }\n      }\n\n      return msg\n    })\n  }\n\n  return msgs\n}\n\nfunction applyCaching(msgs: ModelMessage[], model: Provider.Model): ModelMessage[] {\n  const system = msgs.filter((msg) => msg.role === \"system\").slice(0, 2)\n  const final = msgs.filter((msg) => msg.role !== \"system\").slice(-2)\n\n  const key = providerOptionsKey(model)\n  const providerOptions = {\n    anthropic: {\n      cacheControl: { type: \"ephemeral\" },\n    },\n    openrouter: {\n      cacheControl: { type: \"ephemeral\" },\n    },\n    bedrock: {\n      cachePoint: { type: \"default\" },\n    },\n    [key]: {\n      cache_control: { type: \"ephemeral\" },\n    },\n    copilot: {\n      copilot_cache_control: { type: \"ephemeral\" },\n    },\n    alibaba: {\n      cacheControl: { type: \"ephemeral\" },\n    },\n  }\n\n  for (const msg of unique([...system, ...final])) {\n    const useMessageLevelOptions =\n      model.providerID === \"anthropic\" ||\n      model.providerID.includes(\"bedrock\") ||\n      model.api.npm === \"@ai-sdk/amazon-bedrock\"\n    const shouldUseContentOptions = !useMessageLevelOptions && Array.isArray(msg.content) && msg.content.length > 0\n\n    if (shouldUseContentOptions) {\n      const lastContent = msg.content[msg.content.length - 1]\n      if (\n        lastContent &&\n        typeof lastContent === \"object\" &&\n        lastContent.type !== \"tool-approval-request\" &&\n        lastContent.type !== \"tool-approval-response\"\n      ) {\n        lastContent.providerOptions = mergeDeep(lastContent.providerOptions ?? {}, providerOptions)\n        continue\n      }\n    }\n\n    msg.providerOptions = mergeDeep(msg.providerOptions ?? {}, providerOptions)\n  }\n\n  return msgs\n}\n\nfunction unsupportedParts(msgs: ModelMessage[], model: Provider.Model): ModelMessage[] {\n  return msgs.map((msg) => {\n    if (msg.role !== \"user\" || !Array.isArray(msg.content)) return msg\n\n    const filtered = msg.content.map((part) => {\n      if (part.type !== \"file\" && part.type !== \"image\") return part\n\n      // Check for empty base64 image data\n      if (part.type === \"image\") {\n        const imageStr = String(part.image)\n        if (imageStr.startsWith(\"data:\")) {\n          const match = imageStr.match(/^data:([^;]+);base64,(.*)$/)\n          if (match && (!match[2] || match[2].length === 0)) {\n            return {\n              type: \"text\" as const,\n              text: \"ERROR: Image file is empty or corrupted. Please provide a valid image.\",\n            }\n          }\n        }\n      }\n\n      const mime = part.type === \"image\" ? String(part.image).split(\";\")[0].replace(\"data:\", \"\") : part.mediaType\n      const filename = part.type === \"file\" ? part.filename : undefined\n      const modality = mimeToModality(mime)\n      if (!modality) return part\n      if (model.capabilities.input[modality]) return part\n\n      const name = filename ? `\"${filename}\"` : modality\n      return {\n        type: \"text\" as const,\n        text: `ERROR: Cannot read ${name} (this model does not support ${modality} input). Inform the user.`,\n      }\n    })\n\n    return { ...msg, content: filtered }\n  })\n}\n\nexport function message(msgs: ModelMessage[], model: Provider.Model, options: Record<string, unknown>) {\n  msgs = unsupportedParts(msgs, model)\n  msgs = normalizeMessages(msgs, model, options)\n  if (\n    (model.providerID === \"anthropic\" ||\n      model.providerID === \"google-vertex-anthropic\" ||\n      model.api.id.includes(\"anthropic\") ||\n      model.api.id.includes(\"claude\") ||\n      model.id.includes(\"anthropic\") ||\n      model.id.includes(\"claude\") ||\n      model.api.npm === \"@ai-sdk/anthropic\" ||\n      model.api.npm === \"@ai-sdk/alibaba\") &&\n    model.api.npm !== \"@ai-sdk/gateway\"\n  ) {\n    msgs = applyCaching(msgs, model)\n  }\n\n  // Remap providerOptions keys from stored providerID to expected SDK key\n  const key = sdkKey(model.api.npm)\n  if (key && key !== model.providerID) {\n    const remap = (opts: Record<string, any> | undefined) => {\n      if (!opts) return opts\n      if (!(model.providerID in opts)) return opts\n      const result = { ...opts }\n      result[key] = result[model.providerID]\n      delete result[model.providerID]\n      return result\n    }\n\n    msgs = msgs.map((msg) => {\n      if (!Array.isArray(msg.content)) return { ...msg, providerOptions: remap(msg.providerOptions) }\n      return {\n        ...msg,\n        providerOptions: remap(msg.providerOptions),\n        content: msg.content.map((part) => {\n          if (part.type === \"tool-approval-request\" || part.type === \"tool-approval-response\") {\n            return { ...part }\n          }\n          return { ...part, providerOptions: remap(part.providerOptions) }\n        }),\n      } as typeof msg\n    })\n  }\n\n  return msgs\n}\n\nexport function temperature(model: Provider.Model) {\n  const id = model.id.toLowerCase()\n  if (id.includes(\"qwen\")) return 0.55\n  if (id.includes(\"claude\")) return undefined\n  if (id.includes(\"gemini\")) return 1.0\n  if (id.includes(\"glm-4.6\")) return 1.0\n  if (id.includes(\"glm-4.7\")) return 1.0\n  if (id.includes(\"minimax-m2\")) return 1.0\n  if (id.includes(\"kimi-k2\")) {\n    // kimi-k2-thinking & kimi-k2.5 && kimi-k2p5 && kimi-k2-5\n    if ([\"thinking\", \"k2.\", \"k2p\", \"k2-5\"].some((s) => id.includes(s))) {\n      return 1.0\n    }\n    return 0.6\n  }\n  return undefined\n}\n\nexport function topP(model: Provider.Model) {\n  const id = model.id.toLowerCase()\n  if (id.includes(\"qwen\")) return 1\n  if ([\"minimax-m2\", \"gemini\", \"kimi-k2.5\", \"kimi-k2p5\", \"kimi-k2-5\"].some((s) => id.includes(s))) {\n    return 0.95\n  }\n  return undefined\n}\n\nexport function topK(model: Provider.Model) {\n  const id = model.id.toLowerCase()\n  if (id.includes(\"minimax-m2\")) {\n    if ([\"m2.\", \"m25\", \"m21\"].some((s) => id.includes(s))) return 40\n    return 20\n  }\n  if (id.includes(\"gemini\")) return 64\n  return undefined\n}\n\nconst WIDELY_SUPPORTED_EFFORTS = [\"low\", \"medium\", \"high\"]\nconst OPENAI_EFFORTS = [\"none\", \"minimal\", ...WIDELY_SUPPORTED_EFFORTS, \"xhigh\"]\n\nfunction anthropicAdaptiveEfforts(apiId: string): string[] | null {\n  if ([\"opus-4-7\", \"opus-4.7\"].some((v) => apiId.includes(v))) {\n    return [\"low\", \"medium\", \"high\", \"xhigh\", \"max\"]\n  }\n  if ([\"opus-4-6\", \"opus-4.6\", \"sonnet-4-6\", \"sonnet-4.6\"].some((v) => apiId.includes(v))) {\n    return [\"low\", \"medium\", \"high\", \"max\"]\n  }\n  return null\n}\n\nexport function variants(model: Provider.Model): Record<string, Record<string, any>> {\n  if (!model.capabilities.reasoning) return {}\n\n  const id = model.id.toLowerCase()\n  const adaptiveEfforts = anthropicAdaptiveEfforts(model.api.id)\n  if (\n    id.includes(\"deepseek\") ||\n    id.includes(\"minimax\") ||\n    id.includes(\"glm\") ||\n    id.includes(\"kimi\") ||\n    id.includes(\"k2p\") ||\n    id.includes(\"qwen\") ||\n    id.includes(\"big-pickle\")\n  )\n    return {}\n\n  // see: https://docs.x.ai/docs/guides/reasoning#control-how-hard-the-model-thinks\n  if (id.includes(\"grok\") && id.includes(\"grok-3-mini\")) {\n    if (model.api.npm === \"@openrouter/ai-sdk-provider\") {\n      return {\n        low: { reasoning: { effort: \"low\" } },\n        high: { reasoning: { effort: \"high\" } },\n      }\n    }\n    return {\n      low: { reasoningEffort: \"low\" },\n      high: { reasoningEffort: \"high\" },\n    }\n  }\n  if (id.includes(\"grok\")) return {}\n\n  switch (model.api.npm) {\n    case \"@openrouter/ai-sdk-provider\":\n      if (!model.id.includes(\"gpt\") && !model.id.includes(\"gemini-3\") && !model.id.includes(\"claude\")) return {}\n      return Object.fromEntries(OPENAI_EFFORTS.map((effort) => [effort, { reasoning: { effort } }]))\n\n    case \"@ai-sdk/gateway\":\n      if (model.id.includes(\"anthropic\")) {\n        if \"enabled\",\n              budgetTokens: 16000,\n            },\n          },\n          max: {\n            thinking: {\n              type: \"enabled\",\n              budgetTokens: 31999,\n            },\n          },\n        }\n      }\n      if (model.id.includes(\"google\")) {\n        if (id.includes(\"2.5\")) {\n          return {\n            high: {\n              thinkingConfig: {\n                includeThoughts: true,\n                thinkingBudget: 16000,\n              },\n            },\n            max: {\n              thinkingConfig: {\n                includeThoughts:  effort,\n            {\n              includeThoughts: true,\n              thinkingLevel: effort,\n            },\n          ]),\n        )\n      }\n      return return arr\n      })\n      return Object.fromEntries(\n        copilotEfforts.map((effort) => [\n          effort,\n          {\n            reasoningEffort: effort,\n            reasoningSummary: reasoningEffort: effort }]))\n\n    case \"@ai-sdk/azure\":\n      // https://v5.ai-sdk.dev/providers/ai-sdk-providers/azure\n      if (id === \"o1-mini\") return {}\n      const azureEfforts = [\"low\", \"medium\", \"high\"]\n      if (id.includes(\"gpt-5-\") || id === \"gpt-5\") {\n        azureEfforts.unshift(\"minimal\")\n      }\n      return Object.fromEntries(\n        azureEfforts.map((effort) => [\n          effort,\n          {\n            reasoningEffort: effort,\n            reasoningSummary: \"auto\",\n            include: [\"reasoning.encrypted_content\"],\n   if (model.release_date >= \"2025-11-13\") {\n          arr.unshift(\"none\")\n        }\n        if (model.release_date >= \"2025-12-04\") {\n          arr.push(\"xhigh\")\n        }\n        return arr\n      })\n      return Object.fromEntries(\n        openaiEfforts.map((effort) => [\n          effort,\n          {\n            reasoningEffort: effort,\n            reasoningSummary: https://v5.ai-sdk.dev/providers/ai-sdk-providers/google-vertex#anthropic-provider\n\n      if (model.providerID === \"github-copilot\") {\n        if (model.api.id.includes(\"opus-4.7\")) {\n          return Object.fromEntries([\"medium\"].map((effort) => [effort, { reasoningEffort: effort }]))\n        }\n      }\n\n      if (adaptiveEfforts) {\n        return Object.fromEntries(\n          adaptiveEfforts.map((effort) => [\n            effort,\n            {\n              thinking: {\n                type: \"adaptive\",\n                ...(model.api.id.includes(\"opus-4-7\") || }\n\n      return {\n        high: {\n          thinking: {\n            type: \"enabled\",\n            budgetTokens: Math.min(16_000, Math.floor(model.limit.output / 2 - 1)),\n          },\n        },\n        max: {\n          thinking: {\n            type: \"enabled\",\n            budgetTokens: Math.min(31_999, model.limit.output - 1),\n          },\n        },\n      }\n\n    case \"@ai-sdk/amazon-bedrock\":\n      // https://v5.ai-sdk.dev/providers/ai-sdk-providers/amazon-bedrock\n      if (adaptiveEfforts) {\n        return Object.fromEntries(\n          adaptiveEfforts.map((effort) => [\n            effort,\n            {\n              reasoningConfig: {\n                type: \"adaptive\",\n                maxReasoningEffort: effort,\n                ...(model.api.id.includes(\"opus-4-7\") || model.api.id.includes(\"opus-4.7\")\n                  ? { display: \"summarized\" }\n                  : {}),\n              },\n            },\n          ]),\n        )\n      }\n      // For Anthropic models on Bedrock, use reasoningConfig with budgetTokens\n      if (model.api.id.includes(\"anthropic\")) {\n        return {\n          high: {\n            reasoningConfig: {\n              type: \"enabled\",\n              budgetTokens: 16000,\n            },\n          },\n          max: {\n            reasoningConfig: {\n              type: \"enabled\",\n              budgetTokens: 31999,\n            },\n          },\n        }\n      }\n\n      // For Amazon Nova models, use reasoningConfig with maxReasoningEffort\n      return Object.fromEntries(\n        WIDELY_SUPPORTED_EFFORTS.map((effort) => [\n          effort,\n          {\n            reasoningConfig: {\n              type: \"enabled\",\n              maxReasoningEffort: effort,\n            },\n          },\n        ]),\n      )\n\n    case \"@ai-sdk/google-vertex\":\n    // https://v5.ai-sdk.dev/providers/ai-sdk-providers/google-vertex\n    case \"@ai-sdk/google\":\n      // https://v5.ai-sdk.dev/providers/ai-sdk-providers/google-generative-ai\n      if (id.includes(\"2.5\")) {\n        return {\n          high: {\n            thinkingConfig: {\n              includeThoughts: true,\n              thinkingBudget: 16000,\n            },\n          },\n          max: {\n            thinkingConfig: {\n              includeThoughts: true,\n              thinkingBudget: 24576,\n            },\n          },\n        }\n      }\n      let levels = [\"low\", \"high\"]\n      if (id.includes(\"3.1\")) {\n        levels = [\"low\", \"medium\", \"high\"]\n      }\n\n      return Object.fromEntries(\n        levels.map((effort) => [\n          effort,\n          {\n            thinkingConfig: {\n              includeThoughts: true,\n              thinkingLevel: effort,\n            },\n          },\n        ]),\n      )\n\n    case \"@ai-sdk/mistral\":\n      // https://v5.ai-sdk.dev/providers/ai-sdk-providers/mistral\n      // https://docs.mistral.ai/capabilities/reasoning/adjustable\n      if (!model.capabilities.reasoning) return {}\n      // Only Mistral Small 4 supports reasoning (mistral-small-2603, mistral-small-latest)\n      const mistralId = model.api.id.toLowerCase()\n      if (!mistralId.includes(\"mistral-small-2603\") && !mistralId.includes(\"mistral-small-latest\")) return {}\n      return {\n        high: { reasoningEffort: \"high\" },\n      }\n\n    case \"@ai-sdk/cohere\":\n      // https://v5.ai-sdk.dev/providers/ai-sdk-providers/cohere\n      return {}\n\n    case \"@ai-sdk/groq\":\n      // https://v5.ai-sdk.dev/providers/ai-sdk-providers/groq\n      const groqEffort = [\"none\", ...WIDELY_SUPPORTED_EFFORTS]\n      return Object.fromEntries(\n (adaptiveEfforts) {\n          return Object.fromEntries(\n            adaptiveEfforts.map((effort) => [\n              effort,\n              {\n                thinking: {\n                  type:     },\n          },\n        }\n      }\n      if (model.api.id.includes(\"gemini\") && id.includes(\"2.5\")) {\n        return {\n          high: {\n            thinkingConfig: {\n              includeThoughts: true,\n              thinkingBudget: 16000,\n            },\n          },\n          max: {\n            thinkingConfig: {\n              includeThoughts: true,\n              thinkingBudget: 24576,\n            },\n          },\n        }\n      }\n      if (model.api.id.includes(\"gpt\") || /\\bo[1-9]/.test(model.api.id)) {\n        return Object.fromEntries(WIDELY_SUPPORTED_EFFORTS.map((effort) => [effort, { reasoningEffort: effort }]))\n      }\n      return {}\n  }\n  return {}\n}\n\nexport function options(input: {\n  model: Provider.Model\n  sessionID: string\n  providerOptions?: Record<string, any>\n}): Record<string, any> {\n  const result: Record<string, any> = {}\n\n  // openai and providers using openai package should set store to false by default.\n  if (\n    input.model.providerID === \"openai\" ||\n    input.model.api.npm === \"@ai-sdk/openai\" ||\n    input.model.api.npm === \"@ai-sdk/github-copilot\"\n  ) {\n    result[\"store\"] = false\n  }\n\n  if (input.model.api.npm === \"@ai-sdk/azure\") {\n    result[\"store\"] = true\n    result[\"promptCacheKey\"] = input.sessionID\n  }\n\n  if (input.model.api.npm === \"@openrouter/ai-sdk-provider\" || input.model.api.npm === \"@llmgateway/ai-sdk-provider\") {\n    result[\"usage\"] = {\n      include: true,\n    }\n    if (input.model.api.id.includes(\"gemini-3\")) {\n      result[\"reasoning\"] = { effort: \"high\" }\n    }\n  }\n\n  if (\n    input.model.providerID === \"baseten\" ||\n    (input.model.providerID === \"opencode\" && [\"kimi-k2-thinking\", \"glm-4.6\"].includes(input.model.api.id))\n  ) {\n    result[\"chat_template_args\"] = { enable_thinking: true }\n  }\n\n  if (\n    [\"zai\", \"zhipuai\"].some((id) => input.model.providerID.includes(id)) &&\n    input.model.api.npm === \"@ai-sdk/openai-compatible\"\n  ) {\n    result[\"thinking\"] = {\n      type: \"enabled\",\n      clear_thinking: false,\n    }\n  }\n\n  if (input.model.providerID === \"openai\" || input.providerOptions?.setCacheKey) {\n    result[\"promptCacheKey\"] = input.sessionID\n  }\n\n  if (input.model.api.npm === \"@ai-sdk/google\" || input.model.api.npm === \"@ai-sdk/google-vertex\") {\n    if (input.model.capabilities.reasoning) {\n      result[\"thinkingConfig\"] = {\n        includeThoughts: true,\n      }\n      if (input.model.api.id.includes(\"gemini-3\")) {\n        result[\"thinkingConfig\"][\"thinkingLevel\"] = \"high\"\n      }\n    }\n  }\n\n  // Enable thinking by default for kimi models using anthropic SDK\n  const modelId = input.model.api.id.toLowerCase()\n  if (\n    (input.model.api.npm === \"@ai-sdk/anthropic\" || input.model.api.npm === \"@ai-sdk/google-vertex/anthropic\") &&\n    (modelId.includes(\"k2p\") || modelId.includes(\"kimi-k2.\") || modelId.includes(\"kimi-k2p\"))\n  ) {\n    result[\"thinking\"] = {\n      type: \"enabled\",\n      budgetTokens: Math.min(16_000, Math.floor(input.model.limit.output / 2 - 1)),\n    }\n  }\n\n  // Enable thinking for reasoning models on alibaba-cn (DashScope).\n  // DashScope's OpenAI-compatible API requires `enable_thinking: true` in the request body\n  // to return reasoning_content. Without it, models like kimi-k2.5, qwen-plus, qwen3, qwq,\n  // deepseek-r1, etc. never output thinking/reasoning tokens.\n  // Note: kimi-k2-thinking is excluded as it returns reasoning_content by default.\n  if (\n    input.model.providerID === \"alibaba-cn\" &&\n    input.model.capabilities.reasoning &&\n    input.model.api.npm === \"@ai-sdk/openai-compatible\" &&\n    !modelId.includes(\"kimi-k2-thinking\")\n  ) {\n    result[\"enable_thinking\"] = true\n  }\n\n  if (input.model.api.id.includes(\"gpt-5\") && !input.model.api.id.includes(\"gpt-5-chat\")) {\n    if (!input.model.api.id.includes(\"gpt-5-pro\")) {\n      result[\"reasoningEffort\"] = \"medium\"\n      // Only inject reasoningSummary for providers that support it natively.\n      // @ai-sdk/openai-compatible proxies (e.g. LiteLLM) do not understand this\n      // parameter and return \"Unknown parameter: 'reasoningSummary'\".\n      if (\n        input.model.api.npm === \"@ai-sdk/openai\" ||\n        input.model.api.npm === \"@ai-sdk/azure\" ||\n        input.model.api.npm === \"@ai-sdk/github-copilot\"\n      ) {\n        result[\"reasoningSummary\"] = \"auto\"\n      }\n    }\n\n    // Only set textVerbosity for non-chat gpt-5.x models\n    // Chat models (e.g. gpt-5.2-chat-latest) only support \"medium\" verbosity\n    if (\n      input.model.api.id.includes(\"gpt-5.\") &&\n      !input.model.api.id.includes(\"codex\") &&\n      !input.model.api.id.includes(\"-chat\") &&\n      input.model.providerID !== \"azure\"\n    ) {\n      result[\"textVerbosity\"] = \"low\"\n    }\n\n    if (input.model.providerID.startsWith(\"opencode\")) {\n      result[\"promptCacheKey\"] = input.sessionID\n      result[\"include\"] = LanguageModelV3CallOptions) {\n    const warnings: SharedV3Warning[] = []\n\n    // Parse provider options\n    const compatibleOptions = Object.assign(\n      (await parseProviderOptions({\n        provider: \"copilot\",\n        providerOptions,\n        schema: openaiCompatibleProviderOptions,\n      })) ?? {},\n      (await parseProviderOptions({\n        provider: this.providerOptionsName,\n frequency_penalty: frequencyPenalty,\n        presence_penalty: presencePenalty,\n        response_format:\n          responseFormat?.type === \"json\"\n            ? this.supportsStructuredOutputs === true && responseFormat.schema != null\n              ? {\n                  type: \"json_schema\",\n                  json_schema: {\n                    schema: responseFormat.schema,\n    value: responseBody,\n      rawValue: rawResponse,\n    } = await postJsonToApi({\n      url: this.config.url({\n        path: \"/chat/completions\",\n        modelId: this.modelId,\n      }),\n      headers: combineHeaders(this.config.headers(), options.headers),\n      body: args,\n      failedResponseHandler: this.failedResponseHandler,\n      successfulResponseHandler: createJsonResponseHandler(OpenAICompatibleChatResponseSchema),\n      abortSignal: options.abortSignal,\n      fetch: this.config.fetch,\n    })\n\n    const choice = responseBody.choices[0]\n    const content: Array<LanguageModelV3Content> = []\n\n    // text content:\n    const text = choice.message.content\n    if (text != null && text.length > 0) {\n      content.push({\n        type: \"text\",\n        text,\n        providerMetadata: choice.message.reasoning_opaque\n          ? { copilot: { reasoningOpaque: choice.message.reasoning_opaque } }\n          : undefined,\n      })\n    }\n\n    // reasoning content (Copilot uses reasoning_text):\n    const reasoning = choice.message.reasoning_text\n    if (reasoning != null && reasoning.length > 0) {\n      content.push({\n        type: \"reasoning\",\n        text: reasoning,\n        // Include reasoning_opaque for Copilot multi-turn reasoning\n        providerMetadata: choice.message.reasoning_opaque\n          ? { copilot: { reasoningOpaque: choice.message.reasoning_opaque } }\n          : undefined,\n      })\n    }\n\n    // tool calls:\n    if (choice.message.tool_calls != null) {\n      for (const toolCall of choice.message.tool_calls) {\n        content.push({\n          type: \"tool-call\",\n          toolCallId: toolCall.id ?? generateId(),\n          toolName: toolCall.function.name,\n          input: toolCall.function.arguments!,\n          providerMetadata: choice.message.reasoning_opaque\n            ? { copilot: { reasoningOpaque: choice.message.reasoning_opaque } }\n            : undefined,\n        })\n      }\n    }\n\n    // provider metadata:\n    const providerMetadata: SharedV3ProviderMetadata = {\n      [this.providerOptionsName]: {},\n      ...(await this.config.metadataExtractor?.extractMetadata?.({\n        parsedBody: rawResponse,\n      })),\n    }\n    const completionTokenDetails = responseBody.usage?.completion_tokens_details\n    if (completionTokenDetails?.accepted_prediction_tokens != null) {\n      providerMetadata[this.providerOptionsName].acceptedPredictionTokens =\n        completionTokenDetails?.accepted_prediction_tokens\n    }\n    if (completionTokenDetails?.rejected_prediction_tokens != null) {\n      providerMetadata[this.providerOptionsName].rejectedPredictionTokens =\n        completionTokenDetails?.rejected_prediction_tokens\n    }\n\n    return {\n      content,\n      finishReason: {\n let hasFunctionCall = false\n\n    // map response content to content array\n    for (const part of response.output) {\n      switch (part.type) {\n        case \"reasoning\": {\n          // when         for (const summary of part.summary) {\n            content.push({\n              type: \"reasoning\" as const,\n              text: summary.text,\n              providerMetadata: {\n       break\n        }\n\n        case \"image_generation_call\": {\n          content.push({\n            type: \"tool-call\",\n            toolCallId: part.id,\n            toolName: break\n        }\n\n        case \"local_shell_call\": {\n          content.push({\n            type: \"tool-call\",\n            toolCallId: part.call_id,\n            toolName: \"local_shell\",\n            input: JSON.stringify({ action: part.action } satisfies z.infer<typeof localShellInputSchema>),\n            providerMetadata: {\n              openai: {\n                itemId: part.id,\n              },\n            },\n          })\n\n          break\n        }\n\n        case \"message\": {\n          for (const contentPart of part.content) {\n            if            text: contentPart.text,\n              providerMetadata: {\n                openai: {\n                  itemId: part.id,\n                },\n              },\n            })\n\n sourceType: \"url\",\n                  id: this.config.generateId?.() ?? generateId(),\n                  url: annotation.url,\n                  title: annotation.title,\n                })\n              } else if (annotation.type === \"file_citation\") {\n                content.push({\n                  type: \"source\",\n                  sourceType: \"document\",\n                  id: this.config.generateId?.() ?? generateId(),\n                  mediaType: \"text/plain\",\n                  title: annotation.quote ?? annotation.filename ?? \"Document\",\n                  filename: annotation.filename ?? annotation.file_id,\n                })\n              }\n            }\n          }\n\n          break\n        }\n\n        case \"function_call\": {\n          hasFunctionCall = true\n\n          content.push({\n            type: \"tool-call\",\n            toolCallId: part.call_id,\n            toolName: part.name,\n            input: part.arguments,\n            providerMetadata: {\n              openai: {\n                itemId: part.id,\n              },\n            },\n          })\n          break\n        }\n\n        case \"web_search_call\": {\n          content.push({\n            type: \"tool-call\",\n            toolCallId: part.id,\n            toolName: webSearchToolName ?? \"web_search\",\n            input: JSON.stringify({ action: part.action }),\n            providerExecuted: true,\n          })\n\n          content.push({\n            type: \"tool-result\",\n            toolCallId: part.id,\n            toolName: webSearchToolName ?? \"web_search\",\n            result: { status: part.status },\n          })\n\n          break\n        }\n\n        case \"computer_call\": {\n          content.push({\n            type: \"tool-call\",\n            toolCallId: part.id,\n            toolName: \"computer_use\",\n            input: \"\",\n            providerExecuted: true,\n          })\n\n          content.push({\n            type: \"tool-result\",\n            toolCallId: part.id,\n            toolName: \"computer_use\",\n            result: {\n              type: \"computer_use_tool_result\",\n              status: part.status || \"completed\",\n            },\n          })\n          break\n        }\n\n        case \"file_search_call\": {\n          content.push({\n            type: \"tool-call\",\n            toolCallId: part.id,\n            toolName: \"file_search\",\n            input: \"{}\",\n            providerExecuted: true,\n          })\n\n          content.push({\n            type: \"tool-result\",\n            toolCallId: part.id,\n            toolName: \"file_search\",\n            result: {\n              queries: part.queries,\n              results:\n                part.results?.map((result) => ({\n                  attributes: result.attributes as Record<string, JSONValue>,\n                  fileId: result.file_id,\n                  filename: result.filename,\n                  score: result.score,\n                  text: result.text,\n                })) ?? null,\n            } satisfies z.infer<typeof fileSearchOutputSchema>,\n          })\n          break\n        }\n\n        case \"code_interpreter_call\": {\n          content.push({\n            type: \"tool-call\",\n            toolCallId: part.id,\n            toolName: \"code_interpreter\",\n            input: JSON.stringify({\n              code: part.code,\n              containerId: part.container_id,\n            } satisfies z.infer<typeof codeInterpreterInputSchema>),\n            providerExecuted: true,\n          })\n\n          content.push({\n            type: \"tool-result\",\n            toolCallId: part.id,\n            toolName: \"code_interpreter\",\n            result: {\n              outputs: part.outputs,\n            } satisfies z.infer<typeof codeInterpreterOutputSchema>,\n          })\n          break\n        }\n      }\n    }\n\n    const providerMetadata: SharedV3ProviderMetadata = {\n      openai: { responseId: response.id },\n    }\n\n    if (logprobs.length > 0) {\n      providerMetadata.openai.logprobs = logprobs\n    }\n\n    if (typeof response.service_tier === \"string\") {\n      providerMetadata.openai.serviceTier = response.service_tier\n    }\n\n    return {\n      content,\n      finishReason: {\n        unified: mapOpenAIResponseFinishReason({\n          finishReason: response.incomplete_details?.reason,\n          hasFunctionCall,\n        }),\n        raw: response.incomplete_details?.reason,\n      },\n      usage: {\n        inputTokens: {\n          total: response.usage.input_tokens,\n          noCache:\n            response.usage.input_tokens_details?.cached_tokens != null\n              ? response.usage.input_tokens - response.usage.input_tokens_details.cached_tokens\n              : undefined,\n          cacheRead: response.usage.input_tokens_details?.cached_tokens ?? undefined,\n          cacheWrite: undefined,\n        },\n        outputTokens: {\n          total: response.usage.output_tokens,\n          text: undefined,\n          reasoning: response.usage.output_tokens_details?.reasoning_tokens ?? undefined,\n        },\n        raw: response.usage,\n      },\n      request: { body },\n      response: {\n        id: response.id,\n        timestamp: new Date(response.created_at * 1000),\n        modelId: response.model,\n        headers: responseHeaders,\n        body: rawResponse,\n      },\n      providerMetadata,\n      warnings,\n    }\n  }\n\n  async doStream(options: LanguageModelV3CallOptions) {\n    const { args: body, warnings, webSearchToolName } = await this.getArgs(options)\n\n    const { responseHeaders, value: response } = await postJsonToApi({\n      url: this.config.url({\n        path: \"/responses\",\n        modelId: this.modelId,\n      }),\n      headers: combineHeaders(this.config.headers(), options.headers),\n      body: {\n        ...body,\n        stream: true,\n      },\n      failedResponseHandler: openaiFailedResponseHandler,\n      successfulResponseHandler: createEventSourceResponseHandler(openaiResponsesChunkSchema),\n      abortSignal: options.abortSignal,\n      fetch: this.config.fetch,\n    })\n\n    // oxlint-disable-next-line no-this-alias -- needed for closure scope inside generator\n    const self = this\n\n    let finishReason: {\n      unified: ReturnType<typeof mapOpenAIResponseFinishReason>\n      raw: string | undefined\n    } = {\n      unified: \"other\",\n      raw: undefined,\n    }\n    const usage: {\n      inputTokens: number | undefined\n      outputTokens: number | undefined\n      totalTokens: number | undefined\n      reasoningTokens: number | undefined\n      cachedInputTokens: number | undefined\n    } = {\n      inputTokens: undefined,\n      outputTokens: undefined,\n      totalTokens: undefined,\n      reasoningTokens: undefined,\n      cachedInputTokens: undefined,\n    }\n    const logprobs: Array<z.infer<typeof LOGPROBS_SCHEMA>> = []\n    let responseId: string | null = null\n    const ongoingToolCalls: Record<\n      number,\n      | {\n          toolName: string\n          toolCallId: string\n          codeInterpreter?: {\n            containerId: string\n          }\n        }\n      | undefined\n    > = {}\n\n    // flag that checks if there have been client-side tool calls (not executed by openai)\n    let hasFunctionCall = false\n\n    // Track reasoning by output_index instead of item_id\n    // GitHub Copilot rotates encrypted item IDs on every event\n    const activeReasoning: Record<\n      number,\n      {\n        canonicalId: string // the item.id from output_item.added\n        encryptedContent?: string | null\n        summaryParts: number[]\n      }\n    > = {}\n\n    // Track current active reasoning output_index for correlating summary events\n    let currentReasoningOutputIndex: number | null = null\n\n    // Track a stable text part id for the current assistant message.\n    // Copilot may change item_id across text deltas; normalize to one id.\n    let currentTextId: string | null = null\n\n    let serviceTier: string | undefined\n\n    return {\n      stream: response.pipeThrough(\n        new TransformStream<ParseResult<z.infer<typeof openaiResponsesChunkSchema>>, LanguageModelV3StreamPart>({\n          start(controller) {\n            controller.enqueue({ type: \"stream-start\", warnings })\n          },\n\n          transform(chunk, controller) {\n            if (options.includeRawChunks) {\n              controller.enqueue({ type: \"raw\", rawValue: chunk.rawValue })\n            }\n\n            // handle failed chunk parsing / validation:\n            if (!chunk.success) {\n              finishReason = {\n                unified: \"error\",\n                raw: undefined,\n              }\n              controller.enqueue({ type: \"error\", error: chunk.error })\n              return\n            }\n\n            const value = chunk.value\n\n            if (isResponseOutputItemAddedChunk(value)) {\n              if (value.item.type === \"function_call\") {\n                ongoingToolCalls[value.output_index] = {\n                  toolName: value.item.name,\n                  toolCallId: value.item.call_id,\n                }\n\n                controller.enqueue({\n                  type: \"tool-input-start\",\n                  id: value.item.call_id,\n                  toolName: value.item.name,\n                })\n              } else if (value.item.type === \"web_search_call\") {\n                ongoingToolCalls[value.output_index] = {\n                  toolName: webSearchToolName ?? \"web_search\",\n                  toolCallId: value.item.id,\n                }\n\n                controller.enqueue({\n                  type: \"tool-input-start\",\n                  id: value.item.id,\n                  toolName: webSearchToolName ?? \"web_search\",\n                })\n              } else if (value.item.type === \"computer_call\") {\n                ongoingToolCalls[value.output_index] = {\n                  toolName: \"computer_use\",\n                  toolCallId: value.item.id,\n                }\n\n                controller.enqueue({\n                  type: \"tool-input-start\",\n                  id: value.item.id,\n                  toolName: \"computer_use\",\n                })\n              } else if (value.item.type === \"code_interpreter_call\") {\n                ongoingToolCalls[value.output_index] = {\n                  toolName: \"code_interpreter\",\n                  toolCallId: value.item.id,\n                  codeInterpreter: {\n                    containerId: value.item.container_id,\n                  },\n                }\n\n                controller.enqueue({\n                  type: \"tool-input-start\",\n                  id: value.item.id,\n                  toolName: \"code_interpreter\",\n                })\n\n                controller.enqueue({\n                  type: \"tool-input-delta\",\n                  id: value.item.id,\n                  delta: `{\"containerId\":\"${value.item.container_id}\",\"code\":\"`,\n                })\n              } else if (value.item.type === \"file_search_call\") {\n                controller.enqueue({\n                  type: \"tool-call\",\n                  toolCallId: value.item.id,\n                  toolName: \"file_search\",\n                  input: \"{}\",\n                  providerExecuted: true,\n                })\n              } else if (value.item.type === \"image_generation_call\") {\n                controller.enqueue({\n                  type: \"tool-call\",\n                  toolCallId: value.item.id,\n                  toolName: \"image_generation\",\n                  input: \"{}\",\n                  providerExecuted: true,\n                })\n              } else if            type: \"text-start\",\n                  id: value.item.id,\n                  providerMetadata: {\n                    openai: {\n                      itemId: value.item.id,\n                    },\n                  },\n                })\n              } else if (isResponseOutputItemAddedReasoningChunk(value)) {\n                activeReasoning[value.output_index] = {\n                  canonicalId: value.item.id,\n                  encryptedContent: value.item.encrypted_content,\n                  summaryParts: [0],\n                }\n                currentReasoningOutputIndex = value.output_index\n\n                controller.enqueue({\n                  type: \"reasoning-start\",\n                  id: `${value.item.id}:0`,\n                  providerMetadata: {\n                    openai: {\n                      itemId: value.item.id,\n                      reasoningEncryptedContent: value.item.encrypted_content ?? null,\n                    },\n                  },\n                })\n              }\n            } else if (isResponseOutputItemDoneChunk(value)) {\n              if (value.item.type === \"function_call\") {\n                ongoingToolCalls[value.output_index] = undefined\n                hasFunctionCall = true\n\n                controller.enqueue({\n                  type: \"tool-input-end\",\n                  id: value.item.call_id,\n                })\n\n                controller.enqueue({\n                  type: \"tool-call\",\n                  toolCallId: value.item.call_id,\n                  toolName: providerExecuted: true,\n                })\n\n                controller.enqueue({\n                  type: \"tool-result\",\n                  toolCallId: value.item.id,\n                  toolName: \"web_search\",\n                  result: { status: value.item.status },\n                })\n              } else if (value.item.type === \"computer_call\") {\n                ongoingToolCalls[value.output_index] = undefined\n\n                controller.enqueue({\n                  type: \"tool-input-end\",\n                  id: value.item.id,\n                })\n\n                controller.enqueue({\n                  type: \"tool-call\",\n                  toolCallId: value.item.id,\n                  toolName: \"computer_use\",\n                  input: \"\",\n                  providerExecuted: true,\n                })\n\n                controller.enqueue({\n                  type: \"tool-result\",\n                  toolCallId: value.item.id,\n                  toolName: \"computer_use\",\n                  result: {\n                    type: \"computer_use_tool_result\",\n                    status: value.item.status || \"completed\",\n                  },\n                })\n              } else if (value.item.type === \"file_search_call\") {\n                ongoingToolCalls[value.output_index] = undefined\n\n                controller.enqueue({\n                  type: \"tool-result\",\n                  toolCallId: value.item.id,\n                  toolName: \"file_search\",\n                  result: {\n                    queries: value.item.queries,\n                    results:\n                      value.item.results?.map((result) => ({\n                        attributes: result.attributes as Record<string, JSONValue>,\n                        fileId: result.file_id,\n                        filename: result.filename,\n                        score: result.score,\n                        text: result.text,\n                      })) ?? null,\n                  } satisfies z.infer<typeof fileSearchOutputSchema>,\n                })\n              } else if (value.item.type === \"code_interpreter_call\") {\n                ongoingToolCalls[value.output_index] = undefined\n\n                controller.enqueue({\n                  type: \"tool-result\",\n                  toolCallId: value.item.id,\n                  toolName: \"code_interpreter\",\n                  result: {\n                    outputs: value.item.outputs,\n                  } satisfies z.infer<typeof codeInterpreterOutputSchema>,\n                })\n              } else if (value.item.type === \"image_generation_call\") {\n                controller.enqueue({\n                  type: \"tool-result\",\n                  toolCallId: value.item.id,\n                  toolName: \"image_generation\",\n                  result: {\n                    result: value.item.result,\n                  } satisfies z.infer<typeof imageGenerationOutputSchema>,\n                })\n              } else if (value.item.type === \"local_shell_call\") {\n                ongoingToolCalls[value.output_index] = undefined\n\n                controller.enqueue({\n                  type: \"tool-call\",\n                  toolCallId: value.item.call_id,\n                  toolName: \"local_shell\",\n                  input: JSON.stringify({\n                    action: {\n                      type: \"exec\",\n                      command: value.item.action.command,\n                      timeoutMs: value.item.action.timeout_ms,\n                      user: value.item.action.user,\n                      workingDirectory: value.item.action.working_directory,\n                      env: value.item.action.env,\n                    },\n                  } satisfies z.infer<typeof localShellInputSchema>),\n                  providerMetadata: {\n                    openai: { itemId: value.item.id },\n                  },\n                })\n              } else if (value.item.type === \"message\") {\n                if (currentTextId) {\n                  controller.enqueue({\n                    type: \"text-end\",\n                    id: currentTextId,\n                  })\n                  currentTextId = null\n                }\n              } `${activeReasoningPart.canonicalId}:${summaryIndex}`,\n                      providerMetadata: {\n                        openai: {\n                          itemId: activeReasoningPart.canonicalId,\n                          reasoningEncryptedContent: value.item.encrypted_content ?? null,\n                        },\n                      },\n                    })\n                  }\n                  delete activeReasoning[value.output_index]\n                  if (currentReasoningOutputIndex === value.output_index) {\n                    currentReasoningOutputIndex = null\n                  }\n                }\n              }\n            } else if (isResponseFunctionCallArgumentsDeltaChunk(value)) {\n              const toolCall = ongoingToolCalls[value.output_index]\n\n              if (toolCall != null) {\n                controller.enqueue({\n                  type: \"tool-input-delta\",\n                  id: controller.enqueue({\n                type: \"tool-result\",\n                toolCallId: value.item_id,\n                toolName: \"image_generation\",\n                result: {\n                  result: value.partial_image_b64,\n                } satisfies z.infer<typeof imageGenerationOutputSchema>,\n              })\n            } else if (isResponseCodeInterpreterCallCodeDeltaChunk(value)) {\n              const toolCall = ongoingToolCalls[value.output_index]\n\n              if (toolCall != null) {\n                controller.enqueue({\n                  type: \"tool-input-delta\",\n                  id: toolCall.toolCallId,\n                  // The delta is code, which is embedding in a JSON string.\n                  // To escape it, we use JSON.stringify and slice to remove the outer quotes.\n                  delta: JSON.stringify(value.delta).slice(1, -1),\n                })\n              }\n            } else if (isResponseCodeInterpreterCallCodeDoneChunk(value)) {\n              const toolCall = ongoingToolCalls[value.output_index]\n\n              if (toolCall != null) {\n                controller.enqueue({\n                  type: \"tool-input-delta\",\n                  id: toolCall.toolCallId,\n                  delta: '\"}',\n                })\n\n                controller.enqueue({\n                  type: \"tool-input-end\",\n                  id: toolCall.toolCallId,\n                })\n\n                // immediately send the tool call after the input end:\n                controller.enqueue({\n                  type: \"tool-call\",\n                  toolCallId: toolCall.toolCallId,\n                  toolName: \"code_interpreter\",\n                  input: JSON.stringify({\n                    code: value.code,\n                    containerId: toolCall.codeInterpreter!.containerId,\n                  } satisfies z.infer<typeof codeInterpreterInputSchema>),\n                  providerExecuted: true,\n                })\n              }\n            } else if (isResponseCreatedChunk(value)) {\n              responseId = value.response.id\n              controller.enqueue({\n                type: \"response-metadata\",\n                id: value.response.id,\n                timestamp: new Date(value.response.created_at * 1000),\n                modelId: value.response.model,\n              })\n            } else if (isTextDeltaChunk(value)) {\n              // Ensure a text-start exists, and normalize deltas to a stable id\n              if (!currentTextId) {\n                currentTextId = value.item_id\n                controller.enqueue({\n                  type: \"text-start\",\n                  id: currentTextId,\n                  providerMetadata: {\n                    openai: { itemId:      delta: value.delta,\n              })\n\n              if (options.providerOptions?.openai?.logprobs && value.logprobs) {\n                logprobs.push(value.logprobs)\n              }\n            } else if (isResponseReasoningSummaryPartAddedChunk(value)) {\n              const activeItem =\n                currentReasoningOutputIndex !== null ? activeReasoning[currentReasoningOutputIndex] : null\n\n              // the first reasoning start is pushed in isResponseOutputItemAddedReasoningChunk.\n              if (activeItem && value.summary_index > 0) {\n                activeItem.summaryParts.push(value.summary_index)\n\n                controller.enqueue({\n                  type: \"reasoning-start\",\n                  id: `${activeItem.canonicalId}:${value.summary_index}`,\n                  providerMetadata: {\n                    openai: {\n                      itemId: activeItem.canonicalId,\n                      reasoningEncryptedContent: activeItem.encryptedContent ?? null,\n                    },\n                  },\n                })\n              }\n            } else if (isResponseReasoningSummaryTextDeltaChunk(value)) {\n              const activeItem =\n                currentReasoningOutputIndex !== null ? activeReasoning[currentReasoningOutputIndex] : null\n\n              if (activeItem) {\n                controller.enqueue({\n                  type: \"reasoning-delta\",\n                  id: `${activeItem.canonicalId}:${value.summary_index}`,\n                  delta: value.delta,\n                  providerMetadata: {\n                    openai: {\n                      itemId: activeItem.canonicalId,\n                    },\n                  },\n                })\n              }\n            } else if (isResponseFinishedChunk(value)) {\n              finishReason = {\n                unified: mapOpenAIResponseFinishReason({\n                  finishReason: value.response.incomplete_details?.reason,\n                  hasFunctionCall,\n                }),\n                raw: value.response.incomplete_details?.reason ?? undefined,\n              }\n              usage.inputTokens = value.response.usage.input_tokens\n              usage.outputTokens = value.response.usage.output_tokens\n              usage.totalTokens = value.response.usage.input_tokens + value.response.usage.output_tokens\n              usage.reasoningTokens = value.response.usage.output_tokens_details?.reasoning_tokens ?? undefined\n              usage.cachedInputTokens = value.response.usage.input_tokens_details?.cached_tokens ?? undefined\n              if (typeof value.response.service_tier === \"string\") {\n                serviceTier = value.response.service_tier\n              }\n            } else if (isResponseAnnotationAddedChunk(value)) {\n              if (value.annotation.type === \"url_citation\") {\n                controller.enqueue({\n                  type: \"source\",\n                  sourceType: \"url\",\n                  id: self.config.generateId?.() ?? generateId(),\n                  url: value.annotation.url,\n                  title: value.annotation.title,\n                })\n              } else if (value.annotation.type === \"file_citation\") {\n                controller.enqueue({\n                  type: \"source\",\n                  sourceType: \"document\",\n                  id: self.config.generateId?.() ?? generateId(),\n                  mediaType: \"text/plain\",\n                  title: value.annotation.quote ?? value.annotation.filename ?? \"Document\",\n                  filename: value.annotation.filename ?? value.annotation.file_id,\n                })\n              }\n            } else if (isErrorChunk(value)) {\n              controller.enqueue({ type: \"error\", error: value })\n            }\n          },\n\n          flush(controller) {\n            // Close any dangling text part\n            if (currentTextId) {\n              controller.enqueue({ type: \"text-end\", id: currentTextId })\n              currentTextId = null\n            }\n\n            const providerMetadata: SharedV3ProviderMetadata = {\n              openai: {\n                responseId,\n              },\n            }\n\n            if (logprobs.length > 0) {\n              providerMetadata.openai.logprobs = logprobs\n            }\n\n            if (serviceTier !== undefined) {\n              providerMetadata.openai.serviceTier = serviceTier\n            }\n\n            controller.enqueue({\n              type: \"finish\",\n              finishReason,\n              usage: {\n                inputTokens: {\n                  total: usage.inputTokens,\n                  noCache:\n                    usage.inputTokens != null && usage.cachedInputTokens != null\n                      ? usage.inputTokens - usage.cachedInputTokens\n                      : undefined,\n                  cacheRead: usage.cachedInputTokens,\n                  cacheWrite: undefined,\n                },\n                outputTokens: {\n                  total: usage.outputTokens,\n                  text: undefined,\n                  reasoning: usage.reasoningTokens,\n                },\n                raw: {\n                  input_tokens: usage.inputTokens,\n                  output_tokens: usage.outputTokens,\n                  total_tokens: usage.totalTokens,\n                },\n              },\n              providerMetadata,\n            })\n          },\n        }),\n      ),\n      request: { body },\n      response: { headers: responseHeaders },\n    }\n  }\n}\n\nconst usageSchema = z.object({\n  input_tokens: z.number(),\n  input_tokens_details: z.object({ cached_tokens: z.number().nullish() }).nullish(),\n  output_tokens: z.number(),\n  output_tokens_details: z.object({ reasoning_tokens: z.number().nullish() }).nullish(),\n})\n\nconst textDeltaChunkSchema = z.object({\n  type: z.literal(\"response.output_text.delta\"),\n  item_id: z.string(),\n  delta: z.string(),\n  logprobs: LOGPROBS_SCHEMA.nullish(),\n})\n\nconst errorChunkSchema = z.object({\n  type: z.literal(\"error\"),\n  code: z.string(),\n  message: z.string(),\n  param: z.string().nullish(),\n  sequence_number: z.number(),\n})\n\nconst responseFinishedChunkSchema = z.object({\n  type: z.enum([\"response.completed\", \"response.incomplete\"]),\n  response: z.object({\n    incomplete_details: z.object({ reason: z.string() }).nullish(),\n    usage: usageSchema,\n    service_tier: z.string().nullish(),\n  }),\n})\n\nconst responseCreatedChunkSchema = z.object({\n  type: responseOutputItemAddedSchema = z.object({\n  type: z.literal(\"response.output_item.added\"),\n  output_index: z.number(),\n  item: z.discriminatedUnion(\"type\", [\n    z.object({\n      type: z.literal(\"message\"),\n      id: z.string(),\n    }),\n    z.object({\n      type: z.literal(\"reasoning\"),\n      id: z.string(),\n      encrypted_content: z.string().nullish(),\n    }),\n    z.object({\n      type: z.literal(\"function_call\"),\n      id: z.string(),\n      call_id: z.string(),\n      name: z.string(),\n      arguments: z.string(),\n    }),\n    z.object({\n      type: z.literal(\"web_search_call\"),\n      id: z.string(),\n      status: z.string(),\n      action: z\n        .object({\n          type: z.literal(\"search\"),\n          query: z.string().optional(),\n        })\n        .nullish(),\n    }),\n    z.object({\n      type: z.literal(\"computer_call\"),\n      id: z.string(),\n      status: z.string(),\n    }),\n    z.object({\n      type: z.literal(\"file_search_call\"),\n      id: z.string(),\n    }),\n    z.object({\n      type: z.literal(\"image_generation_call\"),\n      id: z.string(),\n    }),\n    z.object({\n      type: z.literal(\"code_interpreter_call\"),\n      id: z.string(),\n      container_id: z.string(),\n      code: z.string().nullable(),\n      outputs: z\n        .array(\n          z.discriminatedUnion(\"type\", [\n            z.object({ type: z.literal(\"logs\"), logs: z.string() }),\n            z.object({ type: z.literal(\"image\"), url: z.string() }),\n          ]),\n        )\n        .nullable(),\n      status: z.string(),\n    }),\n  ]),\n})\n\nconst responseOutputItemDoneSchema = z.object({\n  type: z.literal(\"response.output_item.done\"),\n  output_index: z.number(),\n  item: z.discriminatedUnion(\"type\", [\n    z.object({\n      type: z.literal(\"message\"),\n      id: z.string(),\n    }),\n    z.object({\n      type: z.literal(\"reasoning\"),\n      id: z.string(),\n      encrypted_content: z.string().nullish(),\n    }),\n    z.object({\n      type: z.literal(\"function_call\"),\n      id: z.string(),\n      call_id: z.string(),\n      name: fileSearchCallItem,\n    localShellCallItem,\n    z.object({\n      type: z.literal(\"computer_call\"),\n      id: z.string(),\n      status: z.literal(\"completed\"),\n    }),\n  ]),\n})\n\nconst {\n            input.push({ role: \"system\", content })\n            break\n          }\n          case \"developer\": {\n            input.push({ role: \"developer\", content })\n            break\n          }\n          case \"remove\": {\n            warnings.push({\n              type: \"other\",\n              message: \"system messages are removed for this model\",\n            })\n            break\n          }\n          default: {\n            const _exhaustiveCheck: never = systemMessageMode\n            throw new Error(`Unsupported system message mode: ${_exhaustiveCheck}`)\n          }\n        }\n        break\n      }\n\n      case \"user\": {\n        input.push({\n          role: \"user\",\n          content: content.map((part, index) => {\n            switch (part.type) {\n              case \"text\": {\n                return { type: \"input_text\", text: part.text }\n              }\n              case \"file\": {\n                if (part.mediaType.startsWith(\"image/\")) {\n                  const mediaType = part.mediaType === \"image/*\" ? \"image/jpeg\" : part.mediaType\n\n                  return {\n                    type: \"input_image\",\n                    ...(part.data instanceof URL\n                      ? { image_url: part.data.toString() }\n                      : typeof part.data === \"string\" && isFileId(part.data, fileIdPrefixes)\n                        ? { file_id: part.data }\n                        : {\n                            image_url: `data:${mediaType};base64,${convertToBase64(part.data)}`,\n                          }),\n                    detail: part.providerOptions?.openai?.imageDetail,\n                  }\n                } else if (part.mediaType === \"application/pdf\") {\n                  if (part.data instanceof URL) {\n                    return {\n                      type: \"input_file\",\n                      file_url: part.data.toString(),\n                    }\n                  }\n                  return {\n                    type: \"input_file\",\n                    ...(typeof part.data === \"string\" && isFileId(part.data, fileIdPrefixes)\n                      ? { file_id: part.data }\n                      : {\n                          filename: part.filename ?? `part-${index}.pdf`,\n                          file_data: `data:application/pdf;base64,${convertToBase64(part.data)}`,\n                        }),\n                  }\n                } else {\n                  throw new UnsupportedFunctionalityError({\n                    functionality: `file part media type ${part.mediaType}`,\n                  })\n                }\n              }\n            }\n          }),\n        })\n\n        break\n      }\n\n      case \"assistant\": {\n        const reasoningMessages: Record<string, OpenAIResponsesReasoning> = {}\n        const toolCallParts: Record<string, LanguageModelV3ToolCallPart> = {}\n\n        for (const part of content) {\n          switch (part.type) {\n            case \"text\": {\n              input.push({\n                role: \"assistant\",\n                content: [{ type: \"output_text\", text: part.text }],\n                id: (part.providerOptions?.openai?.itemId as string) ?? undefined,\n              })\n              break\n            }\n            case \"tool-call\": {\n              toolCallParts[part.toolCallId] = part\n\n              if (part.providerExecuted) {\n                break\n              }\n\n              if (hasLocalShellTool && part.toolName === \"local_shell\") {\n                const parsedInput = localShellInputSchema.parse(part.input)\n                input.push({\n                  type: \"local_shell_call\",\n                  call_id: part.toolCallId,\n                  id: (part.providerOptions?.openai?.itemId as string) ?? undefined,\n                  action: {\n                    type: \"exec\",\n                    command: parsedInput.action.command,\n                    timeout_ms: parsedInput.action.timeoutMs,\n                    user: parsedInput.action.user,\n                    working_directory: parsedInput.action.workingDirectory,\n                    env: parsedInput.action.env,\n                  },\n                })\n\n                break\n              }\n\n              input.push({\n                type: \"function_call\",\n                call_id: part.toolCallId,\n                name: part.toolName,\n                arguments: JSON.stringify(part.input),\n                id: (part.providerOptions?.openai?.itemId as string) ?? undefined,\n              })\n              break\n            }\n\n            // assistant tool result parts are from provider-executed tools:\n            case \"tool-result\": {\n              if (store) {\n                // use item references to refer to tool results from built-in tools\n                input.push({ type: \"item_reference\", id: part.toolCallId })\n              } else {\n                warnings.push({\n                  type: \"other\",\n                  message: `Results for OpenAI tool ${part.toolName} are not sent to the API when store is false`,\n                })\n              }\n\n              break\n            }\n\n            case \"reasoning\": {\n              const providerOptions = await parseProviderOptions({\n                provider: \"copilot\",\n                providerOptions: part.providerOptions,\n                schema: openaiResponsesReasoningProviderOptionsSchema,\n              })\n\n              const reasoningId = providerOptions?.itemId\n\n              if (reasoningId != null) {\n                const reasoningMessage = reasoningMessages[reasoningId]\n\n                if (store) {\n                  if (reasoningMessage === undefined) {\n                    // use item references to refer to reasoning (single reference)\n                    input.push({ type: \"item_reference\", id: reasoningId })\n\n                    // store unused reasoning message to mark id as used\n                    reasoningMessages[reasoningId] = {\n                      type: \"reasoning\",\n                      id: reasoningId,\n                      summary: [],\n                    }\n                  }\n                } else {\n                  const summaryParts: Array<{\n                    type: \"summary_text\"\n                    text: string\n                  }> = []\n\n                  if (part.text.length > 0) {\n                    summaryParts.push({\n                      type: \"summary_text\",\n                      text: part.text,\n                    })\n                  } else if (reasoningMessage !== undefined) {\n                    warnings.push({\n                      type: \"other\",\n                      message: `Cannot append empty reasoning part to existing reasoning sequence. Skipping reasoning part: ${JSON.stringify(part)}.`,\n                    })\n                  }\n\n                  if (reasoningMessage === undefined) {\n                    reasoningMessages[reasoningId] = {\n                      type: \"reasoning\",\n                      id: reasoningId,\n                      encrypted_content: providerOptions?.reasoningEncryptedContent,\n                      summary: summaryParts,\n                    }\n                    input.push(reasoningMessages[reasoningId])\n                  } else {\n                    reasoningMessage.summary.push(...summaryParts)\n                  }\n                }\n              } else {\n                warnings.push({\n                  type: \"other\",\n                  message: `Non-OpenAI reasoning parts are not supported. Skipping reasoning part: ${JSON.stringify(part)}.`,\n                })\n              }\n              break\n            }\n          }\n        }\n\n        break\n      }\n\n      case \"tool\": {\n        for (const part of content) {\n          if (part.type === \"tool-approval-response\") {\n            if (processedApprovalIds.has(part.approvalId)) {\n              continue\n            }\n            processedApprovalIds.add(part.approvalId)\n\n            if (store) {\n              input.push({\n                type: \"item_reference\",\n                id: part.approvalId,\n              })\n            }\n\n            input.push({\n              type: \"mcp_approval_response\",\n              approval_request_id: part.approvalId,\n              approve: part.approved,\n            })\n            continue\n          }\n          const output = part.output\n\n          if (output.type === \"execution-denied\") {\n            const approvalId = (output.providerOptions?.openai as { approvalId?: string } | undefined)?.approvalId\n\n            if (approvalId) {\n              continue\n            }\n          }\n\n          if (hasLocalShellTool && part.toolName === \"local_shell\" && output.type === \"json\") {\n            input.push({\n              type: \"local_shell_call_output\",\n              call_id: part.toolCallId,\n              output: localShellOutputSchema.parse(output.value).output,\n            })\n            break\n          }\n\n          let contentValue: string\n          switch (output.type) {\n            case \"text\":\n            case \"error-text\":\n              contentValue = output.value\n              break\n            case \"execution-denied\":\n              contentValue = output.reason ?? \"Tool execution denied.\"\n              break\n            case \"content\":\n            case \"json\":\n            case \"error-json\":\n              contentValue = JSON.stringify(output.value)\n              break\n          }\n\n          input.push({\n            type: \"function_call_output\",\n            call_id: part.toolCallId,\n            output: contentValue,\n          })\n        }\n\n        break\n      }\n\n      default: {\n        const _exhaustiveCheck: never = role\n        throw new Error(`Unsupported role: ${_exhaustiveCheck}`)\n      }\n    }\n  }\n\n  return { input, warnings }\n}\n\nconst openaiResponsesReasoningProviderOptionsSchema = z.object({\n  itemId: z.string().nullish(),\n  reasoningEncryptedContent: z.string().nullish(),\n})\n\nexport type OpenAIResponsesReasoningProviderOptions = z.infer<typeof openaiResponsesReasoningProviderOptionsSchema>\n",
